According to people from Xinmin, Jin Yutian's unit of the National Salvation Army, led by Zhu Jiqing, is currently stationed near Yingkou Koukou Village, doing its best to protect the area, which has won the favor of the people. More than ten village chiefs have automatically convened and decided to supply Jin's unit with military pay and bullets.

Dai Jimin, Zhu Jiqing's representative, sent a report from Yongji on the 3rd of this month: 1. After the Japanese army occupied Ningguta, they immediately began constructing a military motor road between Ningdun (Dunhua). It was repeatedly attacked and destroyed by the volunteer army, so construction was stopped. However, construction of the railway between Ji (Yanji) and Dun (Dunhua) began simultaneously from both locations in late July, with tunnels being dug in Badian. Many sleepers have been piled up along the way, and steel rails are also being transported one after another. Judging from the situation, it seems they want to complete it before the freezing season. Therefore, the National Salvation Army units of Yang Jingchen, Qiao Xudong, Zhao Yongsheng, Wang Delin, Yu Zuosheng, Ren Fangqiu, etc., are planning to seize the opportunity to vigorously prevent the completion of the road. 2. The Jidong Volunteer Army has been fighting hard for several months without any supplies, and is now in dire need of ammunition, making it difficult to move. There is currently no problem with food, but many crops have been destroyed by artillery fire, which will greatly affect the autumn harvest, and the future is also worrying. 3. During this flood, the dikes upstream of the Songhua River were relatively strong and did not cause major disasters. However, the disaster situation in the Harbin area is extremely severe, unprecedented in decades. The people are displaced and suffering, even more tragically than the Wuhan flood last year.

Shi Pan, the commander of the 13th Route Army of the Volunteer Army, was fighting the Japanese in Suizhong when he was hit by an enemy bullet. He had his left leg amputated at the Pingde German Hospital, fitted with a wooden leg, and was discharged from the hospital last month. He will rush to the front to reorganize his troops and raise supplies in Beijing and Shanghai. Yesterday (9th), he passed through Tianjin from Beijing to Ping. The reporter met him at the station. According to him, the results of this trip were satisfactory. He will prepare winter clothing and bullets for his troops before going to the front. In short, as long as he has a breath, he will vow to kill the enemy to the end. In the past, due to unsuccessful communication, his troops suffered some setbacks. Currently, in addition to Wang Yuwen and Kang Juwu actively contacting each other, he has also obtained considerable contact with Ma Zhanshan, with the aim of recovering his homeland as soon as possible. However, the Northeast aftermath issues and long-term supplies should be given special attention by the people of the country (10th).

On the Way to Central Europe 75

Public · Zhen ·

Investigating Commission Returning by Water

In the clear autumn air, warm sun, and gentle breeze, the League of Nations Investigating Commission, entrusted with a mission of peace, has completed its task and gracefully left China.

The Gange is the smallest of the Italian mail ships. With the League of Nations General Assembly approaching, many distinguished guests gathered, including Lord Lytton, Count Aldrovandi, General McCoy and his wife, and Minister Gu Weijun. Over a hundred people saw them off, including President Wang Jingwei, Ministers Song Ziwen and Luo Wengan, Vice Ministers Liu Chongjie and Xu Mo, and Mayor Wu Tiecheng. It can be said to be a grand occasion. The Italian Minister, Count Galeazzo Ciano, even came from Beiping to see them off, perhaps because the investigating commission was traveling on a ship of his country and he had a responsibility to entertain them. At dinner, the captain had Mrs. McCoy on his right and Minister Gu on his left, with Count Aldrovandi sitting opposite, General McCoy on his right, and Lord Lytton on his left. Aldrovandi also acted like a half-host, emphasizing the importance of national identity.

The investigating commission arrived in Shanghai on March 14th and left Shanghai on September 5th, a period of nearly six months. They traveled nearly 30,000 miles, enduring dust and hardship, rarely staying in one place for long. What they painstakingly compiled is a historical report of over 10,000 words. The content of the report is still kept secret, but some general ideas can be gleaned from private conversations, namely, that the report, in addition to the narration of facts, is able to uphold justice in its conclusions. The three members of the investigating commission originally each had their own positions. It is said that those who have close relations with Japan strongly advocate paying attention to the current situation. After a long period of research and contention with our country's representatives, they set aside the Northeast issue to think for the League of Nations itself. Since it has no power to suppress violence, if it continues to accommodate the present situation, what is the value of this organization, and how can it survive? Therefore, the wording is ultimately cautious.

The Japanese gave the investigating commission a very thorough reception. In terms of material and social facilities, they were far beyond what our country could hope to match. However, the Japanese were insincere, resorting to all sorts of deception, which made the recipients uneasy. It was better to have our country do its best, treat them with sincerity, and gain some goodwill in return. This is something to be thankful for. However, in these past six months, there have been many signs of being stretched thin. In general, legality places the most importance on facts, but from the time of the September 18th Incident until the investigating commission came east, our country was not prepared to collect evidence. The files were incomplete and scattered in Nanjing, Beiping, Luoyang, and other places. The figures were particularly inaccurate. For example, the population of the Northeast, the products that the Northeast supplied to the mainland, and the money that the mainland invested in the Northeast, varied from person to person, and it was not easy to obtain a definite answer. Moreover, scholars in the country were scattered in various places due to livelihood pressures, making it very difficult to solicit opinions. Or they could only write in Chinese, which had to be translated into English and French, or they only knew one part of a problem, which had to be combined with other materials, so the procedures were time-consuming. Also, our country's hotels do not have high-end, luxurious facilities that can accommodate many people. In the end, we had to stay in foreign hotels everywhere. I still remember the Hankou National Hotel, which initially only had four rooms, and then reluctantly added two more, but they were only enough for the investigating commission to rest and work. As a result, Minister Gu wandered around in public rooms all day, receiving guests. The same was true for ships. We could not find them in our country's shipping industry, and we had to abide by their rules when taking foreign ships, which was very inconvenient. In addition to the major ports of Tianjin and Shanghai, there was also a great lack of cars. When passing through Jiujiang, public buses were even used as a substitute, which was laughable. Learn from the past, and it will guide the future. All of these things should be reflected upon. The Chinese delegation supplied the investigating commission with 29 types of written statements, all of which refuted the Japanese's excuses from a legal perspective. At the same time, the investigating commission asked more than a thousand questions about history, geography, personnel, products, and finance, which were answered separately by our side. There were not many public meetings, but Minister Gu had as many as forty private conversations with Lord Lytton, all to clarify issues that had arisen or were about to arise in advance or temporarily. The drafting, translation, and printing of these written statements and answers, as well as the paper and printing costs, were enormous. Each type was printed in 500 or 1,000 copies, both in English and French. At the time, there were no large printing houses that could be responsible for completing the work on time, so we had to go to small printing houses in Tianjin and Shanghai, dividing the work and printing day and night in shifts. The proofreading was hastily gathered on the spot, and the investigating commission was urging us very urgently. It was not until September 2nd that it was finally completed, which was very laborious. Now, they are all packed into wooden boxes and transported with us to Geneva for distribution to the member states of the League of Nations for reference. Those who engaged in the work of the delegation this time were all volunteers. Starting with Minister Gu, each person received a daily stipend of 100 yuan. Therefore, the total cost of travel and sightseeing expenses paid by the delegation was only 220,000 yuan.

Those who accompanied the investigating commission included Secretary Beadle, Cerker, Lord Lytton's personal secretary Easton, and two stenographers. Those who accompanied Minister Gu included Xiao Jirong, counselor of the French embassy, and Chuan Xiaofeng, second secretary. Qian Tai, Yan Deqing, Wang Dazhen, specialized members of the Chinese delegation to Geneva, and Zou Enzhun, secretary. Minister Gu will first go to Paris to submit his credentials and then go to Geneva. Shi Deqian, first secretary of the French embassy, and Xiao Hua, a trainee, will accompany Mrs. Gu to travel abroad next month. Ms. Zhong Xianying, Wang Dazhen's wife, and Ms. Yan Lianying, the wife of military attache Yao Xijiu of the French embassy, will also travel together this time. Ms. Zhong graduated from Bucknell University in the United States and is very proficient in English, always serving as her husband's translator. This is both an internal and external help (Published in Hong Kong on September 7th).

Full Text of the Noulens Case Verdict 76

Defendant: Noulens, male, 34 years old, stateless, currently in custody; Wang Delizeng, female, 36 years old, stateless, currently in custody; Appointed defense attorney, Attorney Chen Ying; The right defendants, in a case of endangering the Republic of China, were prosecuted by the prosecutor, and this court renders the following verdict:

Main Text: Noulens and Wang Delizeng, acting jointly for the purpose of endangering the Republic of China and disrupting public order, are each sentenced to life imprisonment, with deprivation of civil rights for life. The evidence of the crime in the case, three steel boxes, including keys, four envelopes, six yuan eight jiao four fen in silver dollars, eight hundred and twenty-three US dollars, one hundred and fifty Japanese yen, and the original documents, are all confiscated. The remaining parts are acquitted.

Facts: Noulens was originally a member of the Third International Communist Party and was sent by the Third International as the director of the Far East Bureau. He came to China in March of the 19th year of the Republic of China to engage in communist work. He rented houses at No. 235 Sichuan Road, No. 30, Floor C, No. 49 Nanjing Road, No. 74 Hongye Garden, Yuyuan Road, and No. 66 Hart Road in Shanghai for residence and as offices, and rented eight post office boxes, registered four places with the China Wireless Telegraph Bureau for use as communist communications. On one hand, he colluded with traitors Zhu De, Mao Zedong, He Long, etc., and launched large-scale riots in Hunan, Jiangxi and other provinces, devastating the local areas. On the other hand, he divided and transferred the Red Army's Seventh Army, Twentieth Army, and other troops to Tahe (transliterated place name), Xiaoshu (transliterated place name), Fujian, Hunan, Guangdong, and other places to engage in disruption work, attacking the National Army. He also devised a plan to send party members to Nanjing to incite soldiers, mechanics, pilots, guards, and garrison brigades of the Aviation Administration to mutiny in order to increase their own strength. He also suggested preparing Soviet areas at the junction of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei provinces, received money from the Third International, and distributed it to the Southern Bureau, Yangtze River Bureau, Northern Bureau, and Jiangnan Bureau that he had established, inciting farmers, workers, and people to launch a new revolutionary upsurge and initiate class warfare. In addition, he incited workers, disrupted order, and issued slogans such as "Down with the Kuomintang," "Drive out the Kuomintang and the running dogs of imperialism," "Support the Chinese Revolution," and "Support the Chinese Soviet," and so on, which are too numerous to mention. The communist movements in India, the Philippines, the Malay Archipelago, Korea, Annam, Japan, and other places were all under his control. In June of the 20th year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai Public Concession Police learned of this and arrested Noulens on the 15th of the same month in the house at No. 235 Sichuan Road. They then searched the various houses he had rented and used the key hidden on Noulens's body to open the door of Room C-30 at No. 49 Nanjing Road. From the wall cabinet in the room, they took out three steel boxes containing many documents that were evidence of the crime in this case, as well as four envelopes, one containing eight hundred US dollars, one containing twenty-three US dollars, one containing one hundred and fifty Japanese yen, and one containing six yuan eight jiao four fen in silver dollars. Previously, when Noulens was sent as the director of the Far East Bureau, the Third International also sent the female communist Wang Delizeng to monitor the bureau. She lived in the same place as Noulens and participated in confidential matters. When the Shanghai police searched Room C-30 at No. 49 Nanjing Road, they found a note in French on Wang Delizeng, which was an appointment to meet Noulens in the room at 2:00 PM that afternoon. The detectives closed the door from the inside and waited quietly for Wang Delizeng. As expected, she arrived on time, opened the door with her own key, and was arrested as well. The documents of Wang Delizeng and Noulens jointly committing crimes were found in the steel box. Therefore, they were arrested and brought to justice along with the human witnesses. After investigation, the prosecutor of this court filed a public prosecution in accordance with Articles 1, 2, 5, 6, and 10 of the Emergency Law for the Punishment of Endangering the Republic of China, and Article 60, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law.

Reasons: Although Noulens and Wang Delizeng each deny the crime of endangering the Republic of China, the various evidence obtained by this court's investigation is sufficient to fully prove it. The explanations are as follows: 1. Regarding Noulens, the three steel boxes seized in Room C-30 at No. 49 Nanjing Road contain many important documents about the Communist Party. Regarding these documents, one aspect should be the study of the content and records, and the other aspect should be the study of who owns them. The former is the issue of evidence of the crime, and the latter is the issue of the subject of the crime. Now, let us first discuss the evidence of the crime. The documents seized in this case, excluding those involving the Philippines, the Malay Archipelago, Korea, India, Annam, Japan, and other places, only the documents concerning China are sufficient to prove the crime, and there are no less than seventy types (all listed in the A-numbered exhibits). The most prominent ones are as follows: (A) Suggestions to Pia Ai, stating that "At present, the main task of the political parties, the Fourth Army, and the independent divisions organized by our party must be to prepare a Soviet division in the area where Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei provinces meet (approximately Bnsnan Kwangchow, the southwestern part of Anhui, and the northeastern part of Hubei). To achieve this, we must unite the Red Army with the power of ordinary farmers and solve the white army in this area. Before this main force succeeds in solving the white army in this area, the main force of the Red Army must not be sent along the Pinghan Line. Near the railway, farmers and workers must be incited to initiate class warfare and organize small Red Army units to implement a policy of terror against the railway. Farmers can develop their land, approximately in Sinantien and Tienanfu. If the enemy troops voluntarily leave the above-mentioned areas, the Red Army can pursue them with all its strength until they surrender. If the enemy is numerous and the Red Army is defeated, it can take a defensive posture and retreat to its original position if necessary to avoid losing the main force of our army (the rest omitted) (Exhibit A, No. 68, See Exhibit Register No. 2, Page 9) (B) Suggestions on working in the army, such as the above-mentioned strategy, the offensive that we take against the Es area and the position of the Kuomintang army, should be to regard the army of the Kuomintang by means of separation and by means of political tactics. The most important political task of the Communist Party. At present, whether our party's resistance work against attacking the Es area can be fulfilled, especially whether our party's political and organizational work in the army can be carried out diligently, is the turning point. (To be continued)

Important News Two

Central and National Government Memorial Week 77

The Luoyang Provisional Central Party Headquarters and the National Government held Premier Sun Yat-sen Memorial Weeks at 9:00 AM on the 12th in the reception hall of the Central Party Headquarters and the Great Hall of the National Government respectively. The Beijing Office of the Central Party Headquarters also held a memorial week at 9:00 AM. Central Committee members Gu Mengyu, Ye Chucang, Shi Ying, Xiao Jishan, Xiao Zhongzhen, Wang Qi, Li Zonghuang, Fang Juehui, Huang Fusheng, and over 600 staff members attended. After the ceremony led by Chairman Gu Mengyu, Shi Ying reported on the general situation of education in Beijing, stating that the underdevelopment of primary education in Beijing was beyond expectation. According to the statistics of the Beijing Municipal Education Bureau for the 19th year (of the Republic), there were over 77,000 school-age children in the city, but only over 10,000 were in municipal or private primary schools. Most of the children were in private schools, and over 30,000 children in the city were out of school. Therefore, people generally say that it is more difficult to find schooling for their children than to find a job. It is imperative to find ways to provide relief. Starting next semester, 30 simplified compulsory primary schools will be added. Each school will adopt a half-day system, with four grades, each with 50 students, accommodating about 6,000 to 7,000 students. The number of classes in primary schools in Sanpailou and other places will also be increased, which can accommodate another 1,000 students. As for the increased educational expenses, in addition to the start-up fee of over 10,000 yuan, an additional 10,000 yuan will be required each month. If this can be expanded from now on, year by year, then in three or four years, all out-of-school children in the city should have the opportunity to go to school. According to the statistics of the 19th year, the total educational expenses for municipal schools in the city was over 330,000 yuan, and the total number of students in municipal schools was over 12,000, with an average of 27 yuan of educational expenses per student per year. If this is the standard, and if all 30,000 out-of-school children are to receive education, then the educational expenses must increase by nearly one million yuan per year to solve the problem. However, this cannot be achieved with Beijing's current financial resources. Therefore, the addition of simplified compulsory primary schools this time is to provide relief to a large number of out-of-school children with less funding. Not only are public expenses less, but individual burdens are also lighter. This is a manifestation of striving for popularization under the aristocratic education system. As for Beijing's supplementary education, it can be divided into: 1. Establishing mass schools, 2. Preparing for literacy campaigns, 3. Establishing adult supplementary schools, 4. Improving women's vocational supplementary schools, etc., all of which are being actively carried out.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 78

Request to Verify and Collect Land Survey Fees: The people of Songjiang County believe that the provincial order to collect land survey fees for land consolidation at the rate of one dime per mu, with the clause that any amount less than one mu is counted as one mu, not only sets a precedent that has never existed in previous collections, but also violates the principle of equal tax burden. Therefore, county residents such as Yang submitted petitions to the provincial, departmental, and county bureaus, stating that the collection of land price tax and mu donation should be based on the completed mu, verified and remitted according to the established case. There has never been a precedent of rounding up fractions to increase the burden on the people. Moreover, most of the tax amounts on the certificates have fractions of cents, and very few are whole numbers, especially the tax amounts in towns, which are mostly in fractions of cents. If fractions are rounded up, it will inevitably be like draining the pond to catch all the fish, and it will violate the principle of equal tax burden. The people of Songjiang have survived the war, and their savings have been exhausted. Please take into consideration the people's difficulties and still follow the established case for collection, verifying and collecting according to the completed mu for each certificate, so as to eliminate long-standing malpractices and show verification.

Wuxi 79

Zhang Zhongli Inspects Tax Police: Jiangsu Province's anti-smuggling efforts, since being reorganized under the Tax Police Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, have appointed Zhang Zhongli as the director. He has made great efforts to reorganize the anti-smuggling forces and has reorganized the eleven anti-smuggling detachments in the province into eight major districts, which were implemented on September 1st. Recently, Director Zhang felt that it was necessary to personally inspect the reorganized districts. He departed from Shanghai the day before yesterday, first went to Changshu to inspect the officers and police of the seventh district, and finished yesterday. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, he took a boat to Wuxi to inspect the eighth district. Director Chen had already summoned the troops under his jurisdiction to the city to await inspection. After Director Zhang arrived in Wuxi, he stayed at the New World Hotel. Those who came with him included the British advisor Ruston and Secretary Zhang Peide. After a short rest, he began the inspection, addressed the officers and police, and dismissed the old and weak policemen, paying each of them 16 silver yuan. He disbanded them that day. At 6:00 AM this morning, he inspected the merchant patrol team. At around 11:00 AM, he left Wuxi for Zhenjiang to inspect.

Changshu 80

New Education Bureau Director Takes Office: The newly appointed Director of the Education Bureau of this county, Yu Cheng, came to Changshu on the 9th of this month and went to the bureau with the section chief of the county government on the 10th to take over. The original bureau staff members handed over the documents and miscellaneous items, but the handover of financial matters and land properties will continue today (12th).

One Thief Apprehended in Tangjiaqiao Robbery Case: The home of Zhang Pinru in Tangjiaqiao, Jiuzhe District of this county, was robbed last month, with losses of several thousand yuan. At that time, the villagers suspected that it was done by locals and reported it to the Public Security Bureau for close attention. A man named Xiao Guai Laizi was arrested in Wangshi Town, Fushan District, but he was released due to lack of conclusive evidence. After the Tangjiaqiao robbery occurred, Xiao Guai Laizi suddenly changed his behavior and spent lavishly, which aroused unusual attention from the villagers. On the 10th of this month, the team headquarters of the 13th Water Police Team stationed in Meili received a secret report stating that Xiao Guai Laizi was related to the Zhang robbery case in Tangjiaqiao and was hiding in Wangshi Town. The team dispatched six armed policemen to go there, but Xiao Guai Laizi had already fled to Dengshi after hearing the news. The police then went there and arrested Xiao Guai Laizi and escorted him to Meili. It was decided to send him to the Water Police Team headquarters on the 12th to be interrogated by the county.

Jiangyin 81

Fourth National Congress Elects County Executive and Supervisory Committee: The Fourth All-County Representatives Congress had been adjourned twice. After the provincial supervisor Lan Weibin reported to the province, it was discussed and decided by the Provincial Executive Committee to adopt the method of restricting joint nominations and recorded voting. The meeting was held at 3:00 PM on the 10th to elect executive and supervisory committee members. Zhang Gongren of the Provincial Committee supervised the election. Forty-two representatives attended. Eight executive and supervisory committee members were elected. As a result, Chen Xiping (female student of political science and law university), Chen Lan, Xue Dan, Gu Di, and Zhang Xu were elected as executive committee members, Wang Jihua, Tang Kesheng, and Huang Bingying were elected as alternate executive committee members, and Xu Erying, Xu Pinxin, and Chen Jingchen were elected as supervisory committee members, and Cai Peifu was elected as alternate supervisory committee member.

Live Drama of Son Catching Mother in Adultery: Chen Minxiao, the miscellaneous tax director of the Finance Bureau and a native of Ningbo, had been in office for a long time after being appointed by Director Tong. Recently, he was caught in adultery with Lin Guniang, the concubine of Zhang Xiqin in Dukangqiao, a prostitute. Her son, Zhang Zongjian, found out about it and invited his friends Wu Shanbao and Lu Xibao to catch the adulterers late at night (9th). Chen Minxiao fled to the Huayuan Hotel and was caught by Wu and others, who twisted him to the Nancheng Police Station. The patrol chief Zhu Dingyu mediated and fined him ten yuan, plus fifty yuan for all expenses, and the matter was settled. On the 10th, Director Tong Diyi of the Finance Bureau found out about it and dismissed Chen Minxiao. Police Chief Liu Hanzhen of the Public Security Bureau, because Patrol Chief Zhu had arbitrarily penalized the adultery case without reporting to the General Bureau, summoned him to the bureau for interrogation and reprimand.

Nantong 82

Court Completes Processing of Amnesty: The Nantong County Court processed the amnesty and, after review, pardoned more than 30 male and female prisoners, including Qian Xia, etc. The number of male and female prisoners whose sentences were reduced totaled more than 350, including Liu Hongsheng, etc. All the processing has been completed and reported to the High Court.

Expanding and Building the Coastal Naval Engineering Road: In the area where the two counties of Tonghai border, the ports of Da'an, Lao, and Hong are often frequented by sea bandits. Because of inconvenient transportation, when the military and police go to suppress them, the bandits have already fled far away. It has now been decided by the joint defense zone to expand and build a road along the coast to reach various ports to facilitate defense and suppression. The military engineers will be used to expand and build the road.

Red and White Pills Abound in Tong County: Red and white pills are selling very well in the urban and rural areas of Tong County, and their harm is endless. There are indeed manufacturing organizations in the urban and rural areas. These poisonous pills are transported and sold to Yancheng and other places. The organizers have great power, so they have not been caught yet.

Military Police Search for Weapons in Bandit Areas: Banditry in the eastern townships of Nantong is gradually subsiding. Currently, the military police, accompanied by informants, are searching for weapons and ammunition buried by the bandits in the bandit areas such as Yiyu to eliminate future troubles.

Danyang 83

Three Bandits Executed by Shooting: The bandits Jiang Xisan, Chen Zhulin, and Dai Fugui had repeatedly committed serious robbery cases. They were arrested by the county government detectives one after another. After interrogation, they confessed their crimes. The provincial government was immediately telegraphed for instructions. The provincial government telegraphed back to allow the death penalty. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Shen Cheng of the county government proposed the criminals by name, bound them, and took them to the execution ground for execution by shooting.

Three Kidnappers Apprehended: Yesterday, three bandits were sipping tea in the Hongfu Teahouse in the South Gate. A tea guest caught sight of them carrying pistols, but dared not speak out at the time. After the bandits left, he reported to the plainclothes detective Xu Mingtou, who followed them to Dongmen Street and arrested the three bandits. Two Browning pistols were found on them. They were immediately sent to the county government. After interrogation by Shen Cheng, they were identified as Tang Dakun, Tang Xiaokun, and Tang Laosan from Houxu Village. They confessed to having committed a kidnapping case in Bailong Temple in the northern countryside. Shen Cheng, based on the confession, ordered them to be detained for further handling.

Gaoyou 84

Resumption of Jiangbei Long-Distance Bus Service: The Jiangbei long-distance bus service was suspended during the great flood last year and has been suspended for a year. Now, because the Yun embankment has been repaired, the old office address of the bureau was destroyed by the water last autumn. Now, a private house at the mouth of Miaoxiang Lane has been rented as an office, and it is scheduled to resume service on the 14th of this month.

Police Second Squad Captures Three Bandits: Shi Xingrui, the leader of the Second Squad of the police stationed in Tajizhen, the twelfth district, received a secret report from Xie Weiguan, a town resident, the day before yesterday, stating that bandits were hiding in Jiagou Town. He led a team to the town and captured Guo Rongkui. After interrogating him, he confessed that the theft case of Yang Peizhu in Jiagou was committed by Wang Zaifu, Wang Zailu, and Chen Youzhang. Team Leader Shi immediately led a team to arrest them, but the Wang brothers had already fled after hearing the news. Only Chen Youzhang was captured. According to Chen's confession, the case was committed by Wang Zailu, Yang Xi, and others. Then, Yang Xi was captured. He was escorted to the city last night (9th) and sent to the county government for interrogation through the police team.

Pinghu 85

Xinmin Theater Destroyed: The Xinmin Theater in Beisi Nei was losing money and decided to lease it to the newly organized Gongle Company for business. Another opera troupe was hired to perform on the night of the 10th. When the opera started that day, some public officials went to see it. The gatekeeper insisted on buying tickets, and they left displeased. At night, the theater was packed. Before the opera was half over, three men in short coats and trousers rushed in from outside the door and grabbed the Shandong gatekeeper and beat him severely. At this time, about fifty or sixty accomplices, who had been lying in wait upstairs and downstairs, responded in unison and threw teapots and chairs at the stage and first-class seats. The order was disrupted, and people fled out the door. At the same time, a group of troublemakers came from across the river west of the theater, looking for the foreman to beat him. They mistakenly grabbed the son of Shen Hengbo, the former director of the Jiangxi Tax Bureau in this city, and beat him with wood, causing him to be covered in blood. The people in the theater fled. The three gatekeepers and Shen were seriously injured and have gone to the county to seek examination.

Outline of the Plan to Improve Jiangsu Normal Education 87

(Two)

Article 11: Improve the level of normal education. The measures are as follows: A. The appointment of normal school teachers should be based on the principle of having received normal education training. B. Encourage normal school teachers to pursue further studies, especially focusing on the research of teaching methods. C. Improve the level of each subject, enhance educational effectiveness, and strictly examine academic performance. D. Implement the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, supplement them with reference to local special needs. E. Strictly conduct entrance examinations. F. Conduct graduation comprehensive examinations to evaluate the quality of students' academic performance as one of the standards for evaluating school principals.

Article 12: Focus on the basic training of normal education, divided into moral education and teaching, listed as follows: 1. Regarding moral education, A. Training of individual personality, implement the moral education standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, especially focusing on cultivating the habit of hard work, self-reliance, enduring hardship, and hard work. B. Training of citizenship, especially cultivating the spirit of mutual assistance, cooperation, sacrificing private interests, and serving the society. C. Training of daily life and work, should focus on the implementation of labor operations, physical exercise, and average exercise, to cultivate healthy habits, in order to be suitable for primary school education. 2. Regarding teaching, A. Focus on the research of the subject itself and the cultivation of production skills, avoiding the malpractice of empty talk about teaching methods. B. Focus on the production of simple instruments and the collection of specimens on the spot, reducing the difficulties in teaching in rural areas in practice. C. Focus on teaching practice. If the practice credits are not fulfilled, even if the academic performance is qualified, they cannot graduate. The implementation of the practice method should follow the curriculum standards of the high school normal science promulgated by the Ministry of Education, but special attention should be paid to the practice of composite teaching.

Article 13: Enrich the equipment of normal education, and attention should be paid to the following items: A. The various books that should be prepared in the library should be suitable for reference to the normal education curriculum. B. The science experiment laboratory should be equipped with various applied instruments and specimens. C. Various necessary equipment for farms or factories. Article 14: This outline will be announced and implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education and reported to the Provincial Government for consultation and filing with the Ministry of Education. (End)

Changes in Directors of Baoshan and Jiading Education Bureaus 88

Since the January 28th Incident, the losses in the counties of Songhu were great, especially in Baoshan and Jiading. Pu Wengui, the director of the Baoshan Education Bureau, and Yang Shiceng, the director of the Jiading Education Bureau, resigned one after another because of the lack of educational funding and the difficulty of handling affairs. Jiading County has appointed Shui Kangmin as the successor, who has already taken office. Baoshan has appointed Feng Guohua to take over. Both of them graduated from the Second Normal School and are both intelligent and capable. Feng had previously been appointed as the director of the Chongming Education Bureau but declined the position. He is currently handling social education in Zhenjiang and has achieved considerable success. Regarding the Baoshan Bureau Director position, he is still declining politely.

Local News

Provisional Standards Promulgated by the Ministry Should Be Followed Before the Curriculum Standards Are Issued 89

The Municipal Education Bureau Instructed All Primary Schools Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau instructed the municipal and private primary schools in this city yesterday, stating that recently, various schools have inquired of the bureau whether they should still implement the old standards for this semester, as the curriculum standards are being revised, according to newspaper reports. After investigation, these new standards have not yet been issued. The curriculum for this semester should still be handled in accordance with the provisional standards. In addition, the Bureau previously listed four points of attention that should be followed when arranging the daily class schedule and ordered the schools to follow them. Now, when arranging the daily class schedule, they should be revised, copied, and issued, so that the schools can follow them. This order copies and issues the points of attention that should be followed when arranging the daily class schedule for primary schools.

Points of Attention That Should Be Followed When Arranging the Daily Class Schedule for Primary Schools 90

1. Before the Ministry of Education promulgates the official primary school curriculum standards, the names of the subjects should absolutely follow the provisional standards promulgated by the Ministry.

2. The time for each subject should be calculated in minutes and should not exceed or decrease by more than 10% of the standards promulgated by the Ministry.

3. The arrangement of the daily class schedule should pay attention to the following points: 1. In the lower grades, 30 minutes per period should be the principle. 2. In the middle and upper grades, each period should not exceed 60 minutes at most. 3. For subjects that require practice, the number of classes should be more, and the time for each class should be shorter. 4. Knowledge classes or subjects that require a lot of brain power should be scheduled for the first period in the morning and should not be scheduled for the periods before and after lunch. 5. For subjects that take a lot of time to clean up, such as crafts, two periods should be combined, or they should be scheduled for the last period of each day to save time. 6. Physical education classes should not be scheduled for the period before lunch or the period after lunch. 7. The arrangement of each subject should be evenly distributed throughout the week according to the amount of time. 8. Labor and mental subjects should be evenly harmonized and allocated every day.

4. Other principles regarding the arrangement of the daily class schedule should be adopted as much as possible within the possible range.

Minutes of the Shanghai County Education Bureau Affairs Meeting 91

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 258th Bureau Affairs Meeting yesterday afternoon. Those present were Director Shi, Inspector Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Yang Huiming, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Zheng Shaoyuan, Qian Zhonghou, Xi Siwu, Shen Jingzhi, and Wu Jianqing. Director Shi presided over the meeting, and Pan Sheng recorded the meeting. The formalities were performed as usual. Report matters (omitted). Discussion matters: 1. The case of Tangwan Primary School requesting the allocation of funds to build school buildings. It was resolved that no funds could be allocated, and the request should be delayed. 2. The case of the principal of Tangwan Primary School requesting to adjust the salary level. It was resolved that the salary should be paid according to the third-level, second item of the salary standard for primary school principals in this county (monthly payment of 36 yuan). 3. The case of the principal of the Rural Teachers' Junior High School requesting the refund of the discounted salaries of the school's faculty and staff for the 20th year. It was resolved that the County Education Association should be handled in accordance with the fifth resolution of the previous meeting. 4. The case of the Xinxing People's Education Center requesting the allocation of repair funds. It was resolved that no funds could be allocated and should be handled by the center within the possible scope of its regular expenses. 5. The case of Tangwan Primary School requesting to exchange school land to add to the school site and build walls. It was resolved that the matter was feasible, but the case involved changes to school property and should be reported for approval before handling. 6. According to the report of the principals' meeting in the third district, there are private schools and church schools that conflict with laws and regulations in the school district, please find a way to ban them. It was resolved that all schools should report the hindering situation in detail before further handling.

Jinan University Started Classes Yesterday 92

President Zheng Hosted All Faculty and Staff at the Hua'an Building

The National Jinan University held its opening ceremony in the Zhiyuan Hall of the school at 7:30 AM yesterday (12th). About a thousand faculty members and students attended, gathered together in one hall. After performing the formalities, President Zheng gave a sincere speech and reported on the process of restoration since the war, stating that after the January 28th Incident, the students were scattered in various places, so schools were established in Shanghai, Guangdong, and Jiangsu to hold classes, and borrowing students were accepted to help the out-of-school youths in the war zones. The total losses of the school were no less than 800,000. Only 30% to 50% of the funding was issued after the war, in addition to maintaining the three schools in Shanghai, Guangdong, and Jiangsu, and part of it was saved for reorganization needs. A postwar reorganization committee was established to plan the restoration. The initial reorganization was completed on August 25th. The entire university students gradually moved back since August 29th, and the old view gradually recovered. After that, strict training should be carried out to improve and enforce production education. The courses offered are all important and rarely repeated, and the level is improved, focusing on the cultivation of basic intelligence, so that they can meet the needs of the society in the future. He also urged that special investigations and researches should be added to the overseas Chinese issues so that the overseas Chinese students can solve the difficulties of the overseas Chinese elders after returning. After the ceremony, the class officially started, and all the teachers and students were in a very happy spirit.

At 3:00 PM, President Zheng, on behalf of all the students and parents, hosted a tea party for all the faculty and staff at the 8th floor of the Hua'an Building. During the meeting, President Zheng stood up and gave a speech, stating that "all professors have a long history with Jinan and are very grateful for their earnest teachings to the students on weekdays. Since January 28th, all the teachers and students have been able to move back to Zhenru and restore the original state in the turbulent flow, which is the result of everyone's efforts. In the future, we should establish the teaching profession and improve the learning style to change the atmosphere and establish the great spirit of the highest institution." The meeting ended happily around 5:00 PM.

In addition, the list of professors, deans, and department heads for the 21st year of the school had been appointed earlier and reported in various newspapers. Later, the two colleges of Education and Law were merged, resulting in slight changes. Free Talk

One Branch of Discussion

The Assassin Named Zheng 102

— Zhan Lu

An assassin named Zheng said: "I am killing this traitor for the sake of the world, and I will not regret dying." This assassin was Zheng Huchen, who lived in the Song Dynasty. He once killed Jia Sidao at the Mian'an Temple in Zhangzhou, which is a memorable event in past history.

Another assassin named Zheng said: "He came to die, and I risked killing him. First, to glorify the party and the country, second, to glorify the revolution, third, to eliminate harm for Shandong, and fourth, to avenge my uncle. Now that the great revenge has been avenged, I have long disregarded my life and death." This assassin was Zheng Jicheng, who lives in modern times. He recently killed Zhang Zongchang at the Jinan Railway Station, which is a memorable event in modern history.

The words spoken by both assassins were selfless dedication to eliminate harm for the people. How慷慨激昂! Those who believe in karma may suspect that the modern Zheng Jicheng is the reincarnation of Zheng Huchen of the Song Dynasty. However, Zhang Zongchang's qualifications for evil are not comparable to Jia Sidao. Sidao not only harmed the country but also betrayed it. Zongchang was a perverse warlord who actually understood that betraying the country was not a business, and he refused to use the title of his ancestor Zhang Bangchang. This person still had a glimmer of clarity. After his death, most people applauded, but a small number of people still lamented for him? They lamented that his awakening came too late. Zheng Huchen killed Jia Sidao and also died under the law. Zheng Jicheng killed Zhang Zongchang, I wonder if he can be granted leniency? In Mian'an Temple in Zhangzhou, later generations erected a stone stele with the inscription "Song Zheng Huchen killed Jia Sidao here." According to Minzhong Fuwen, I wonder if anyone will erect a stone stele near the Jinan Railway Station with the inscription "Republic of China Year 21, Zheng Jicheng killed Zhang Zongchang here?" These are all future events, no need to predict, we can only wait and see?

God's Random Talk 103

— Hong Liu

The British scholar Spencer said: "The missionary holds the Bible in one hand and tells us very kindly: "We must be charitable. When others hit our left cheek, we must also turn our right cheek to bear it. Resistance is barbaric, revenge is a sin! We must be docile, as docile as sheep, and God will give you eternal happiness!" But when his country is at war with another country, he will grit his teeth and tell us: "We must rise up! Take our guns and aim at our enemies! We must use iron and blood to win our final victory!" Many people think this is a very contradictory thing, but in fact, it is very logical: he tells us to be charitable for the sake of human survival, and he tells us to fight with the enemy for the sake of human survival: in the world, this is the same need."

Therefore, for us Western civilized people, wherever a missionary goes, there will be a fearsome warship following him, opening up with dignified authority. This is very reasonable. We are not like that. Morality has always had no boundaries. He tells you to be kind and tolerant in dealing with people. When a robber holds a steel knife against your neck, he still tells you to be kind and tolerant. If you move even a little, we civilized Westerners will scold you for being barbaric, for being a semi-civilized person. Don't say that General Zhang's non-resistance policy is a timeless wonder, it is the most civilized behavior in the world!

National Salvation Should Be Divided into Two Major Groups 104

— Yuan Wenxin

"Struggle, self-determination, bloodshed!"

In this critical moment of life and death, we can no longer speak empty words. The enemy's ambition for aggression has long been revealed. What is justice, what is peace? We can only bleed, we can only struggle, we can only self-determine!

My meaning is to divide the compatriots of the whole country into two major groups. One group immediately goes to fight, and the other group endures death to nurture the orphans of this Republic of China.

For those who die first, there is certainly the spirit of "the head can be broken, but the will cannot be bent," but for those who die later, the responsibility is more important, the work is more difficult, and they must not fail the obligation of entrusting orphans to those who die first.

We who want to be those who die later must have the following goals: First, we must recognize the enemy and not be used or seduced by them, and do things "with one heart and one mind" based on our conscience.

Second, we must support those who die first, encourage those who die first, and comfort those who die first, so that they can kill the enemy with peace of mind.

Third, we must not be greedy, lazy, selfish, or cause trouble ourselves, and intensify our obligations.

Compatriots! Isn't the enemy's flag still flying in the Northeast? Isn't the sound of resistance from the Northeast Volunteer Army lengthening day by day? I am one who dies first, I am one who dies later, and I will quickly do it according to my own wishes! Compatriots! Work hard! Work hard!

A National Salvation Plan 105

— Xu Yi

"Whether the country survives or not? It depends on whether you can implement it."

1. Principles

Production: Machine production. Concentrate engineering talents and build machines ourselves. Immigrate and colonize the borders, plant forests and build roads to alleviate the excess of labor.

Consumption: Use less foreign goods, ride cars less, watch movies less, and go to dance halls less. Weddings and funerals should all be simplified.

Distribution: It is important to be even. The rich should do more charitable work, such as helping the poor and elderly, and caring for widows and orphans.

2. Second Degree Work

Agriculture: Promote rural governance, practice group defense, improve agricultural products, and equalize land rights. Industry: Formulate labor laws and regulations, implement worker education, and improve the manufacturing of domestic goods.

Commerce: Sever economic ties with Japan and focus on honest transactions.

Learning: Focus on academic research, raise moral standards, implement physical training, and participate in practical work.

Soldiers: Born to die, deeply understand the righteousness, not greedy for merit, not discouraged. Officials: Do not take a single thing from the people, do not waste a single penny of public money.

Women: Save money and food, and go to the national crisis together.

Autumn Butterfly News 106

— Zi Wei

"Zheng Zhengqiu and Hu Die take the stage"

Autumn Butterfly is not a butterfly in autumn, but two famous figures in the art world.

Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu is a pioneer in performing vernacular dramas and a famous director of the Star Film Company. His words have long been praised by the general public.

Ms. Hu Die has been publicly honored as the Film Queen. In the Chinese film industry, she is definitely a modern girl who has no equal. There are too many people who care about and are fascinated by her.

Now, these two will cooperate in the Mid-Autumn Festival to perform a newly compiled vernacular drama in response to the times. The name is "The Substitute Wife." You think: this is really going to make people happy, because Zheng has not been on stage for a long time. As for Hu Die, her beautiful face and charming voice on the screen have long made people itchy and itchy in their ears, wishing to see her.

Talks in the "睇嚮齋" 107

— Gan Yi

Chen Sanli

Chen Sanli's fame as a poet is known throughout the world, and his prose is also the same. His poems have the charm of the Tang and Song dynasties, and his prose follows the style of Fang and Yao, matching Ma Qichang. His style name is Boyan, and he is from Yining, Jiangxi. He served as a principal of the Ministry of Personnel after passing the imperial examination. During the Wuxu coup, his father, Douzhen, was the governor of Hunan. He accompanied his parents in Changsha and participated in the new policies. He often discussed reforms with the investigating censor Huang Gongdu (Zunxian) and the education envoy Xu Yanfu (Renqing). Therefore, the political affairs of a province were implicitly in Chen Sanli's hands, and his father firmly believed in him. When the matter failed, Douzhen was dismissed, and Chen Sanli was stripped of his official position and never used again. Later, he was elected by his fellow villagers as the general manager of the Nanxun Railway. Chen Sanli was upright and impatient with the drama, so he resigned. He paid taxes on a house in Baimen and entertained himself with poetry in his old age. Jiang Governor Duan Wuqiao (Fang) always liked to be close to famous scholars, especially valuing Chen Sanli's character. He invited him to his staff and was about to recommend him to the court. Chen Sanli showed his unwillingness, acting with lonely loyalty, unparalleled at the time. This year he is eighty years old, lying high in Kuanglu. Even the slightest correspondence is rarely shared with others, and his淡曠 is very similar to the people of the Wei and Jin dynasties. As the Japanese bandits are rampant, the government has formed a national crisis meeting, including Chen Sanli. The authorities have written his name in large characters in the newspapers and invited him to receive the certificate. Alas! This is because they do not know Chen Sanli's ambition. Chen Sanli is devoted to the mountains and rivers, not seeking fame in the late Qing Dynasty, not happy to rely on the Hongxian Dynasty, not participating in conspiracies during the Restoration, and not wanting to criticize the warlords in the autumn. To say that he would come out into the world during the heyday of party rule, I do not believe it. He has written several volumes of "Sanyuan Jingshe Poems," and the world calls him the Sanyuan Elder.

Original Appearance

This is truly an opportunity. The Central Grand Theater on the Mid-Autumn Festival will be packed again. It is said that the newly published "Good News" is preparing a special issue for "The Substitute Wife."

Group 108

— A Jie

"Good Noun? Bad Noun?"

In the Chinese dictionary, the word "group" is the most auspicious noun: like the attainment of cohabitation love between two sexes, it is called reunion: a rich friend is called a "round-faced rich man." The ancients said: "On the fifteenth day of August, the daughter returns to Ning, and on that day she returns to her husband's house, which is called the Reunion Festival." In the Qing Dynasty, it was customary for officials to congratulate each other during festivals and celebrate together, which was called "group worship." Isn't the word "group" an auspicious noun? What else is "團花" "good flowers and full moon" which is not auspicious: therefore, it is customary in society to eat rice balls and golden balls during the Spring and Autumn festivals and celebrations, isn't it to take the beautiful meaning of reunion? Now, everything is really upside down. Since the establishment of the "Blood Soul Elimination Group," what "Iron Blood Elimination Group," "Conscience Elimination Group," "Hot Blood Punishment Group," "Thunderbolt Killing Group," "Blood Drip Shoveling Group":::: etc., someone has counted that there are more than sixty groups in total. The round-faced evil merchants, upon hearing the word "group," are all panic-stricken, their hearts and livers chilled, just like the Wuxi people's "spinning around." Newspaper advertisements and notices are a complete mess. Alas! In the eyes of evil merchants, isn't this group the most hateful bad noun?

Silver Threads (12) 109

— Jiang Hongjiao

(6)

Mr. Wang spoke these few words, then opened the door and left. Just as he was about to open the door, Fenruo once again urged him that if he went to the meeting place, he must not reveal that Regiment Commander Yuan was at her house.

"The meeting place is buzzing with discussion, because they can't find the commander anywhere. Which road did the commander come from, how is it that no one in the town saw him? Ah! Today, the whole town is welcoming the commander like mad. It's a pity that this sister-in-law is unable to attend because she is taking care of the madman upstairs." Mr. Wang said this to Regiment Commander Yuan again before leaving.

"Okay! You go first, I want to go upstairs and see the patient, and then I'll go to the meeting." Regiment Commander Yuan's intention was to urge Mr. Wang to leave quickly, but he had many words in his heart that he wanted to carefully and intimately discuss with Fenruo.

"Then, goodbye, Commander! You must comfort that madman well. It's a pity that besides this sister-in-law, everyone here hates and dislikes him. He also has the surname Yuan, perhaps he's a relative of the commander's:::" Mr. Wang still hesitated slowly.

"Mr. Wang, if you go to the meeting place immediately, you might meet Dr. Zhang, so please notify him that after the meeting, he must come here to give him an injection. Mr. Wang, please do me the favor!" Fenruo said, and then opened the door and very politely saw Mr. Wang out. In reality, these few words were equivalent to issuing an eviction notice. Mr. Wang also felt that there was no point in lingering any longer. However, after Mr. Wang left Fenruo's door, he was very disappointed and full of suspicion. He wondered why he had never heard them mention any relationship with Regiment Commander Yuan. Regiment Commander Yuan had never been here before or after the war? It's true that the madman Yuan is a Yuan, and the commander's surname is also Yuan, and the madman, when he was mad, said that Regiment Commander Yuan was her husband. Could this be true? If they are husband and wife, how could Regiment Commander Yuan leave her here and not care about her at all? If it's true, Fenruo must have a close relationship with the Yuan family, no doubt. Fenruo is a widow, perhaps she has some kind of ambiguous relationship with Regiment Commander Yuan? That would make me disappointed. How can a poor merchant like me compare with a rich and noble commander? But, if Fenruo really has an ambiguous relationship with the commander, how could she be so poor? If there is no ambiguous relationship, why would she immediately want to rush me out now, and Fenruo looks very flustered, which is very suspicious.

The more Mr. Wang thought about it, the more jealous he became of Regiment Commander Yuan, and he also resented You Fenruo. He was plotting to reveal this secret at the meeting place, at least to sweep the commander's reputation and prestige to the ground. But then he thought again, and he became timid. He negotiated with himself. He is a military man, no matter what, I can't fight him. If he wants to act rashly and pull out his pistol, I'm a sacrifice. If he wants to act civilly, he'll use some excuse to arrest me, say I'm a Communist, and sentence me to death. I have no way to appeal my injustice. In any case, I can't offend him.

He slowly walked step by step to his house, and did not go to the meeting place. He was very sad, very indignant, and very annoyed, but he dared not make a decision.

Guomin News Agency reports that, according to Finance Minister Song Ziwen's announcement, today's newspapers reported foreign affairs regarding the Japanese seizing salt taxes, sending notes to the United States, Britain, and France, the content of which is quite inaccurate. The total amount of foreign debt funds seized by the Japanese, as of August 31, is approximately 1,746,100 yuan. The note stated that this kind of seizure of foreign debt funds is sufficient to harm the security of the foreign debts guaranteed by salt taxes, which is very obvious. It was found that in September of this year, a large amount of payment was due, and this seizure by the Japanese also harms the National Government's ability to pay other debts. Now, in view of the fact that your citizens hold bonds guaranteed by salt taxes, we ask your governments to pay attention to the serious situation caused by the seizure of the salt affairs audit offices in the Eastern Three Provinces, etc. Minister Song also denied the government's consideration of extending the payment of various amounts due in September, saying that the Salt Affairs Audit Office has already issued instructions to allocate the interest due in September, totaling 45,000 pounds for British and French foreign debts, 115,000 pounds for the Crisp Loan, and the principal due, totaling 250,000 pounds for British and French foreign debts. However, Minister Song also strongly stated the difficulty the government faces in paying debts after the Japanese seized the loan funds. At a time when the national government will continue to do its best to maintain the credit of the debts guaranteed by salt taxes, the Japanese warlords have seized funds that should belong to the bondholders for six months and refuse to release them. Moreover, when they seized the salt affairs audit offices earlier, they stated that they should at least remit the amount to be repaid as usual. Now they have immediately gone back on their word, which is extremely unfair, it is said.

Supporting the League of Nations Covenant Association Cables League of Nations Member States 131

Japanese Destruction of Territorial Integrity of Member States

Please Advocate Unanimously Based on the Spirit of the Covenant

The League of Nations Covenant Support Committee, initiated by over seventy trade associations in this city, has recently heard that the number of participating trade associations has exceeded one hundred and twenty. It is actively implementing measures for economic blockade against Japan for several days. In order to awaken the attention of various countries in the world, a special cable was sent to the member states of the League of Nations, requesting unanimous economic blockade against Japan based on the spirit of the Covenant. The original cable reads: To the representatives of all member states of the League of Nations, Japan's former Minister of the Army, Nan Jiro, said to people when he went to the Eastern Three Provinces to inspect on December 20 last year, "From now on, only the issue of one regime remains. This incident is actually a revolution in Manchuria. Its purpose is to drive out the old regime." On January 6 this year, Nan Jiro arrived in Moji from the Eastern Three Provinces and said to Japanese reporters that according to the current situation in Manchuria, there should be three most important principles: one of which is the independence of Manchuria. This is because Japan suddenly occupied the Eastern Three Provinces by force and created a puppet organization, breaking away from Chinese rule. As evidenced by the remarks of the Minister of the Army, it was all created by him single-handedly. It is absolutely impossible to deceive the world with national self-determination. This action by Japan is clearly in violation of Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant, which states, "The member states should respect and preserve the territorial integrity of all member states." Recently, it has even publicly announced its recognition of the puppet organization, which is tantamount to tearing up Article 10 of the Covenant and challenging all member states. According to Article 10 of the Covenant, if the territorial integrity of a member state is violated, the League of Nations Executive Council should plan to fulfill the method of this obligation. The intention of this article is that when the territorial integrity of a member is violated, the Executive Council should unite the strength of all members to jointly safeguard it, in other words, to jointly sanction the aggressor. For a year, the League of Nations has not taken decisive and effective measures, which is nothing more than because there are many affairs in Europe and a sanction is added, and it is feared that the dispute will expand and affect the overall situation. I do not know that today's affairs, like a person suffering from sores, are easier to heal if cut early, and fostering carbuncles will definitely cause trouble. If Japan occupies the Eastern Three Provinces and its power is consolidated in three to five years, then the Pacific War will be difficult to avoid. It is better to sanction it as soon as possible, which is easier to deal with. This is not for the sake of our country alone, but for the sake of the overall situation of the world. If the League of Nations cannot handle it strictly in accordance with the spirit of the Covenant after receiving the report of the Investigation Team, then international authority will be completely destroyed by the Japanese, and once a bad example is set, Europe will also have many affairs from now on. Therefore, the Shanghai 70-odd trade associations have initiated the formation of this association, gathering national commercial organizations, upholding the spirit of supporting the League of Nations Covenant, and based on the principle of freedom of trade for merchants, to carry out economic blockade against Japan in advance and automatically. We hope that various countries in the world will not hesitate to sympathize and provide assistance. League of Nations Covenant Support Committee Koushou.

Chairman Lin's Speech 133

Reporting on Various Domestic and Foreign Affairs Issues

Central News Agency reports that Chairman Lin was in Shanghai and did not go out yesterday morning. In addition to receiving Mayor Wu and old friends around 9:00 a.m., he also received reporters from various news agencies near noon and reported on various domestic and foreign affairs issues that the people of the country have been paying attention to recently. Around 1:00 p.m., he went out to visit friends again and had not returned to his residence by late evening. The points discussed by Chairman Lin are recorded on the left.

Wang Will Go to Beijing Soon: Chairman Lin said that he had met with President Wang a few days ago and had a pleasant conversation. Mr. Wang's illness has subsided, but the fever has not completely subsided. He will return to Beijing as soon as he recovers, but there is no fixed date yet. Mr. Wang has always been responsible and will not show any negative attitude at this time of national crisis. Urge Chen to Cancel Leave: Minister of Communications Chen Mingshu visited him the morning before yesterday. He said that Chen's leave had expired, so he urged him to return to Beijing to assume his duties immediately. The reporter then asked the Chairman whether there were other important tasks to ask Chen to be responsible for. Chairman Lin replied that Chen had previously resigned from his duties to the central government, but it was not approved, so Chen will of course still be the Minister of Communications when he returns to Beijing. However, Chen has not yet indicated whether or not he can.

Reorganize Fujian Province: Regarding the reorganization of Fujian Province, Chairman Lin told reporters that he had not heard of this matter, and the central government has no such proposal. He has only seen this record in the newspapers recently. However, the people of Fujian Province have indeed petitioned the government to reorganize Fujian Province, and he also hopes that the government can actively rectify it so that the politics of Fujian Province can be brought on track.

Third Plenary Session Date: The Third Plenary Session has been decided to be postponed, because at this time of high autumn and fat horses, it is the time for the country to use troops. The government is now actively suppressing bandits, and Chairman Chiang and other central committee members are all with the army. If they rush back to attend, it may have a major impact on military affairs. Moreover, previous plenary sessions have also been postponed to March or half a year.

Diplomacy with Japan: The reporter then asked whether it was true that our Ambassador to Japan, Chiang, was ordered to visit the Japanese Minister of the Army and Minister of Foreign Affairs and proposed a so-called compromise, as reported in yesterday's newspapers. Chairman Lin replied that this is a diplomatic issue and can be inquired of the diplomatic authorities. However, this is a Reuters telegram and may not be completely reliable. I hope you will not trust it lightly.

National Participation in Politics: Regarding the progress of national participation in politics, Chairman Lin said that the draft regulations have been drafted by Mr. Wang Jingwei and others and are still being carefully reviewed. Because these regulations are related to the election of the people, the government should take a serious attitude to avoid misunderstandings in various provinces due to competitive elections.

Recovering Lost Territory: I believe that recovering the lost territory in the Northeast is something that the government should do, and the people should also eagerly hope that the government can announce a concrete plan and hope that the government can proceed in an orderly manner to achieve the goal. However, this plan is not only related to military affairs and cannot be announced, but also has a great impact on international relations, so although the government has made a decision, it cannot be announced lightly to comfort the people and cause unexpected disputes. As for ordering the suppression of rebels, it is originally a paper order that can be issued at any time, but all preparations are not easy, but the government should actively prepare, not be afraid of difficulties, to achieve this goal.

Sun Will Go North Soon: Mr. Sun Zhesheng will arrive in Shanghai on the 23rd of this month. I hope that Mr. Sun will also go to Beijing to participate in national affairs. Mr. Hu Zhantang's illness has gradually improved. It is not known whether Mr. Wu Tiyun will come to Shanghai with Sun Zhesheng.

Lin Will Return to Beijing Soon: After discussing various important issues, Chairman Lin further inquired in detail about the work of the reporters and sincerely exhorted them, and his words were concerned. Finally, he said that he would stay in Shanghai for three or four days and then return to Beijing. After the conversation, the reporters resigned, and Chairman Lin sent them out of the door.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Resolves on Opinions on Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan 134

Reply by Letter After Approval by the Executive Committee

Regarding the issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan, since Vice President Chen of the Central Bank, in the name of the Research Committee Chairman, proposed three points that should be studied: 1. The weight and fineness of the new silver coins; 2. The ratio of silver taels to silver coins for contracts still in effect; 3. What measures should be taken to make the general public understand and trust this change? The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various groups were sent letters separately to solicit opinions. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce then sent letters to various trade associations and local chambers of commerce to solicit opinions widely, and organized a research committee on the issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan to study the principles of currency system, domestic commercial conditions, and responses from various parties in detail. After several meetings, the last committee meeting was convened yesterday, and the following opinions were resolved:

First Question: The weight and fineness of the new coins should be determined based on the principle of not violating the following four principles. The so-called four principles are: 1. If the fineness of the currency is too high, it is easy to privately melt and destroy it; if the fineness is too low, it is easy to induce private minting. As evidenced by the precedent of currency, it is necessary to prevent the occurrence of these two malpractices when deciding on the weight and fineness. 2. The main coin is unlimited legal tender, which is different from the limited legal tender of the auxiliary coin, so the nominal price of the auxiliary coin can be higher than the actual price, while the nominal price and actual price of the main coin cannot be far apart. 3. Under the current circumstances, the government's minting of coins should not be allowed to lose money, but it should not be hoped for surplus, because once there is a surplus, hard currency can also be issued indiscriminately like soft currency, resulting in currency inflation and soaring prices. In the history of currency in our country, such precedents can be counted. 4. Changes and adjustments in regulations should be made within the possible scope so that the social and economic situation does not have drastic changes. Second Question: For silver tael contracts that are still in effect, those who fulfill their debts after the abolition of taels and the change to yuan will naturally pay new national currency, and the new value of the new national currency will be the fairest conversion ratio. Because after the abolition of taels, there is no so-called ocean cent market price, and there is no other standard for conversion other than the actual price of this national currency.

Third Question: In order to make society understand and trust, 1. Society should be made more convenient to use silver yuan than to use silver taels, or at least have the same convenience as silver taels. The conditions are: (A) For free minting, anyone who holds old coins, yuanbao, or silver bars, the national mint can respond to their request at any time and pay the same amount of new national currency at the announced conversion rate. (B) For freedom of transportation, the prohibitions that previously prohibited the transportation of cash out of the country and restricted the transportation of cash out of the country should not be easily promulgated by local authorities, but should be handled carefully by the Central Bank, which is responsible for regulating finance, at any time. 2. Society should be made to regard silver yuan as silver taels and have the same accurate fineness so that there is no fear of inferior coins and light coins disturbing the mind. The conditions are: (A) Recalling old coins and reminting them at any time. (B) Centralizing minting power, not only should the Hangzhou factory set up by the central government be abolished, but also the private silver yuan bureau set up by the military in Sichuan Province and the mint set up in Guangzhou should be ordered to stop with strict orders, so as not to be out of reach, or only mint hao yang and ignore it. (C) Organizing a currency system supervision committee, selecting a number of people from commercial organizations and the financial community across the country to take turns stationed in Shanghai to supervise the division of labor. Their tasks are to participate in the verification of hard currency, to announce its fineness at any time, and after the verification in Shanghai, important cities can also set up verification departments by commercial organizations to verify at any time for comparison and to facilitate credit. Secondly, participate in the public inspection of soft currency to announce its reserve ratio at any time. The main purpose of this article is to publicize the task of supervising the currency system to the whole country, and not to be set up in Shanghai, but to be the exclusive responsibility of the people of Shanghai, in order to awaken the belief of the whole country with an attitude of great justice and selflessness, so that the new currency system can be easily implemented.

The above opinions will be sent by the committee to the standing committee for submission to the executive committee for approval before a formal reply is sent.

Director of the Seawall Project Reports to the Construction Department
