Liquidation of Data Bank 136

Savings Deposits of 70,000 Yuan to be Paid Out Starting Today

According to the Kuo Wen News Agency, the Data Bank on Beijing Road officially announced its dissolution yesterday, and has engaged Accountant Xie Lin and Lawyer Qiu Fenling to handle the winding-up and liquidation. The reasons for the bank's dissolution and the subsequent arrangements are detailed below:

Established Last Year The bank was established in March of last year with a paid-up capital of 500,000 yuan. Huang Mingdao served as the general manager, and Tang Haishan as the manager, handling all banking operations. From the outset, business flourished. In the first four months of the first half of last year, profits amounted to approximately 60,000 yuan.

Reasons for Liquidation In addition to operating pawn loans, the bank also dealt in large quantities of government bonds. After the September 18th Incident in the Northeast, bond prices plummeted. Subsequently, with the outbreak of the January 28th Shanghai Incident, four or five out of ten of the bank's shareholders suffered losses on government bonds. Hopes for a price recovery were dashed due to the unstable situation, making it impossible to recoup losses. Although the board of directors resolved to raise new capital on August 27th of this year, various factors prevented its realization. The bank's savings deposits totaled only about 70,000 yuan, while the credit side, such as loans and pawn loans, amounted to approximately 200,000 yuan. To avoid significant losses, all the bank's shareholders reluctantly decided to cease operations and liquidate at a meeting on the 11th of this month.

Social Stability A reporter from the Kuo Wen News Agency, concerned that the liquidation of the Data Bank might affect the social economy, visited a prominent figure in the banking sector. According to him, the Data Bank was not a member of the Bankers Association. The bank ceased operations due to poor management and the impact of falling government bond prices. It is reported that the savings portion of the internal deposits will be repaid in full. Because the amount is not significant, it is not expected to have any impact on society.

Savings to be Repaid The bank closed its doors yesterday morning, with a notice posted in front stating: "Notice: As resolved by the shareholders' meeting yesterday, the bank is to be dissolved and liquidated. All savings department deposits are entrusted to the Zhengze Accounting Firm for payment (4th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road). Other debts are entrusted to Lawyer Qiu Fenling and Accountant Xie Lin as representatives for liquidation (5th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road). Data Bank Co., Ltd., September 13, 21st Year." Accountant Xie Lin also issued a notice stating: "Notice: The Data Bank is ceasing operations and liquidating. All savings department deposits, having been established with the approval of the Ministry of Finance, are being handled separately. This accountant has been entrusted to make payments of the original principal. Therefore, all depositors of the Data Bank's savings department are notified to bring their deposit passbooks to the Zhengze Accounting Firm, 4th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road, between 10:00 AM and 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM and 3:00 PM daily, starting from September 13th, to collect their funds."

Report to the Court After implementing the liquidation, Lawyer Qiu and Accountant Xie reported to the First Special District Court for record yesterday and jointly issued a liquidation notice stating: "Notice: The shareholders' meeting of Data Bank Co., Ltd. resolved to cease operations and dissolve for liquidation from September 12th. This lawyer and accountant have been entrusted as liquidators. In addition to reporting to the competent court, all depositors are hereby notified to bring their deposit passbooks to this accountant's office for registration between 9:00 AM and 11:00 AM daily starting from September 19th. Furthermore, all debts owed to the bank must be paid in full to this accountant's office by September 30th. Qiu Law Firm, 5th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road, Shanghai. Xie Accounting Firm, 4th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road, Shanghai."

Huang Mingdao's Illness The reporter drove to the residence of Huang Mingdao, the general manager of the bank, yesterday, but due to Huang's severe lung ailment, he was unable to receive visitors. According to his family, Huang has been unable to attend to bank affairs since the September 18th Incident last year, due to illness, and is therefore quite out of touch with current matters.

Accountant's Statement Accountant Xie Lin, who is handling the case, stated that the bank's capital was 500,000 yuan and it was a limited company registered with the Ministry of Industry and holding a license. Since its opening last year, business had been excellent. However, it was subsequently affected by the September 18th Incident and the Shanghai War, resulting in significant losses due to the large number of government bonds purchased. They勉强supported the business until now, but not only was the share capital completely lost, but there were also debts that could not be paid. Yesterday, the shareholders held a meeting and decided that they could not continue operations, and then they passed a resolution to dissolve the company, as well as appoint this accountant and Qiu Fenling as liquidators. They are currently taking over accounting documents, and they are scheduled to register the bank’s debts from September 19th, and collecting the issued loans at the same time to balance the bank’s income. However, the savings department deposits were originally submitted to the Ministry of Finance for independent operation, and according to the Savings Bank Rules, directors and managers must bear unlimited liability. The business has been paid by the directors, and it has been entrusted to this accountant to pay the funds at this office from the 13th, with a total of about 70,000 yuan, and an announcement was made, which will be published tomorrow.

Bank's Aftermath For the sake of carefulness, the bank convened an extraordinary general meeting of shareholders on September 11th, with more than 30 attendees (out of a total of about 70 shareholders), exceeding more than half of the people. The public elected Tang Mangong as the chairman, and the meeting unanimously decided to stop operations and liquidate. The bank’s house is rented, and it can be returned after cleaning up. All 30 employees were dismissed immediately after the shareholders’ meeting on the 11th, and they were given three months’ severance pay. Only a few personnel were left to handle the closure. It is reported that the bank does not owe any money to the same industry, and the amount of all credit exchanges, in addition to the thousands of dollars outside the issuance of loans and personnel, is about 20,000 yuan. After all the funds are recovered, it will be enough to pay for the various expenses, and there will be no losses.

Tonghua Steamer Runs Aground in Qizhou 138

All Crew and Passengers Stranded Without Food

Two Ships Dispatched to Tow

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tonghua steamer, en route from Nanjing to Wuhan, ran aground upstream of Qizhou. The Jiangshun steamer attempted to rescue it, but was unsuccessful. Two more ships have now been dispatched to tow it. The details of the incident are as follows:

Circumstances of the Grounding The Tonghua steamer set sail from Nanjing on the afternoon of the 8th. On the night of the 10th, it sailed to a point ten li upstream of Qizhou. Due to the rising tide and turbulent waters, and the pilot's negligence, it entered a shoal, and the hull ran aground. The riverbed on both sides of the area is covered with thick sand and mud, and the Tonghua steamer's hull is stuck in the shoal. The captain attempted to reverse the engines, but was unable to move the vessel. He had no choice but to send a telegram requesting assistance.

Jiangshun's Towing The company's Jiangshun steamer, upon receiving the report, immediately sailed to the scene of the accident to tow the Tonghua. However, the grounding was too deep, and despite repeated attempts to tow the vessel, it was impossible to dislodge it. The Jiangshun then telegraphed the Shanghai office, requesting that another vessel be dispatched for rescue.

Food Shortages The Tonghua steamer, traveling from Nanjing to Hankou, carried only three days' worth of provisions. There were more than one hundred armed comrades among the passengers, along with the entire crew, totaling more than two hundred people. After the grounding, they expected to arrive in Hankou on the 11th, but they were unable to arrive on schedule, and the food supply was exhausted, resulting in a lack of meals. The captain, Qiang Sheng, telegraphed the Shanghai office again yesterday morning, requesting that food supplies be sent quickly to provide relief.

Two Ships to Rescue Upon receiving the report, the Shanghai office's shipping department director, Wang Tong, telegraphed the Hankou branch yesterday morning, ordering the Lilong steamer, which was on the Hunan route, to be immediately dispatched to Qizhou for rescue. At the same time, the Tunan steamer, which was en route from Beijing to Hankou, was also ordered to proceed to Qizhou to assist in the towing operation. As for the food needed by the Tonghua steamer, the Tunan steamer was instructed to provide supplies to prevent the crew and passengers from going hungry.

Telephone Subscribers Must Pay According to New Regulations Today 139

Subscribers' Association Holds Emergency Meeting to Discuss Countermeasures

The Telephone Subscribers' Association held an emergency meeting yesterday, as today is the deadline for paying fees under the new regulations.

Yesterday's Meeting The Shanghai Special District Telephone Subscribers' Association held its third emergency meeting of all directors yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Attendees included Cai Qiaojun, Yu Xiji, Zhou Fuzhang, Cao Zhigong, Hu Fengxiang, Wang Weiying, Zhang Yichen, and others. Hu Fengxiang was elected chairman, and Zheng Dongshan recorded the minutes. The meeting began with a report on letters received from various parties and replies from the telephone company. The next item on the agenda was a discussion on how to respond to the telephone company's deadline of the 13th for fee collection. The following resolutions were adopted: 1. Send a letter to the telephone company stating that the new regulations are not yet fully understood and requesting that they be translated into Chinese for detailed discussion and verification. Until a resolution is reached, please do not disconnect the lines. 2. If the company rashly disconnects the lines, the company shall be fully responsible for all losses incurred as a result. 3. Appoint Hu Fengxiang, Yu Xiji, and Cao Zhigong to negotiate with the company. 4. Appoint Zhou Fuzhang and Zhang Xianfang to liaise with the Public Works Bureau. 5. Appoint Li Weiliang and Wang Zhaocheng to liaise with the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association. 6. Appoint Cai Qiaojun and Qiu Jialiang to liaise with the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the International Settlement. 7. Schedule another emergency meeting for 5:00 PM on the 13th of this month (i.e., today). 8. If the company fails to provide a satisfactory response, adopt the most stringent measures to deal with the situation (the measures are confidential). 9. Notify subscribers that if the company forcibly disconnects the lines, they should lodge a serious protest. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.

Letter to the Company To Whom It May Concern: We have received and read your three letters. After the investigations, regardless of anything else, we feel that we can not afford the increased telephone fees. We feel that it is important to consult about the matter. Our association held an emergency meeting yesterday, and it was felt that with regard to your company's newly revised general rules, there is an urgent need to translate them into Chinese, and publish them to the Chinese telephone users. This should be done before we research the rules again and discuss how to cooperate. The people are asked to not to cut the wires prior to the resolution, in order to avoid other disputes. Appoint Hu Fengxiang, Yu Xiji, Cao Zhigong, the three of you will go forward. We ask you to grant the connections.

Notice to Subscribers Notice is hereby given regarding the opposition to the increase in telephone charges. Our association has repeatedly sent letters to the company and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, strictly requesting negotiation on file. We have now received a reply from the company, agreeing to translate the new regulations into Chinese for publication, but making no specific statement regarding the price increase. The society convened a meeting yesterday and decided to send representatives to the company immediately for serious negotiations. We will be unable to cut the wires before the issue is resolved. In the event that the company disregards reason and forcefully cuts the lines or pursues payment, subscribers should maintain a calm attitude and await the impartial resolution of the law, in order to consolidate unity and facilitate progress. This is what we hope for.

Tian Tong's Coffin Transported to Hubei Yesterday 141

Moved to Jianghua Steamer Yesterday Afternoon

Sets Sail for Hankou at 2:00 AM This Morning

Tian Tong (Zi Qin), a veteran member of the Kuomintang and former member of the National Government Committee, passed away in Shanghai in the autumn of the 19th year. His coffin was placed in the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association on Manufacturing Bureau Road. Later, the Central Executive Committee decided on a public burial, and the National Government ordered the Hubei Provincial Government to handle the matter. The provincial government immediately established a preparatory office and scheduled the public burial to be held in Hubei on the 20th of this month. Director He Chengjun and Mayor Wu of this city, along with Social Affairs Bureau Director Wu Xingya, discussed and decided to use the Jianghua steamer for transportation. White silk arches were erected in advance at the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association, Jinliyuan Wharf, and on the Jianghua steamer, with white banners reading "Meritorious Service to the Party and the Nation" hanging on them. Banners on the steamer read "Mr. Tian Ziqin's Coffin Transported Back to Hubei for Public Burial." Zhang Shuhou and others from the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai and the Anhui Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai held a public memorial service at the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association yesterday. Chen Haosheng of the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association presided over the service, which was filled with grief. At 3:00 PM yesterday, Tian's coffin was transported from the Hubei Fellow-Townsmen Association. Leading the procession was a white lantern with the words "Four Virtues Hall Tian's High Illumination." Following were the military band and armed military police dispatched by the municipal government, lining up in a single file. Among the mourners were Ju Zheng, Zhang Ji, Zhou Daoyu, Yang Shukan, Wu Tiecheng, Wu Xingya, and representatives from various agencies and organizations, numbering in the dozens. Last in the procession was Tian's coffin carriage, drawn by four black horses, along with a car carrying Tian's portrait and a wooden memorial tablet. At 5:00 PM, the procession arrived at the wharf. Amidst the mournful sounds of the military band, eight pallbearers carried the coffin onto the Jianghua steamer, placing it in the reserved middle cabin. Tian's wife and sons, Tian Qiao, Tian Yan, and Tian Xiu, followed behind, weeping sorrowfully. After the coffin was properly placed, Tian's family members, relatives, and friends paid their respects before departing. Family members distributed two copies of the "Taiping Magazine," edited by Tian, as souvenirs. It is reported that the Jianghua steamer is scheduled to set sail for Hankou at 2:00 AM this morning (the 13th).

Social Affairs Bureau Calls Various Industries for Discussions on Promoting Factory Inspections 146

Since the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau began implementing factory inspections in this city on September 1st, various industries have requested postponement due to the decline in industry and commerce after the war. The bureau has scheduled meetings with various organizations to provide detailed explanations. The details are as follows:

Notification to Various Industries The Social Affairs Bureau notified various industrial and commercial organizations in this city yesterday, stating: "Notice is hereby given that there are many misunderstandings regarding the items that should be inspected in accordance with the law during the initial implementation of factory inspections by this bureau. As a result, many have requested postponement. Therefore, it has been specifically decided to invite various industrial and commercial organizations to provide detailed explanations at 2:00 PM on the afternoons of September 14th and 15th to dispel concerns. At that time, it is hoped that your association will send two or one representatives to the bureau on time to listen to the discussions. This notice is hereby given. Wu Xingya, Director, September 12th, 21st Year of the Republic of China."

Discussion Schedule At 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 14th, the Shanghai National Products Factory Association, the Machinery-Made National Products Factory Association, the China Industrial Federation, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the Chinese Cotton Mill Association will each send two representatives. At 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 15th, the Chinese Soap Guild, the Chinese Woolen Mill Guild, the Knitting Industry Guild, the Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Industry Guild, the Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Mill Guild, the Egg Factory Industry Guild, the Silk Factory Industry Guild, the Chinese Cigarette Industry Guild, the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Guild, the Copper and Iron Machinery Industry Guild, the Flour Industry Guild, the Cosmetics Industry Guild, the Lighter and Cotton Ginning Industry Guild, the Tin Printing and Can Making Industry Guild, the Refining Industry Guild, the National Products Rubber Products Industry Guild, and the Enamelware Industry Guild will each send one representative. The location is the Social Affairs Bureau at Xiaonanmen.

Explanation of Doubts The Social Affairs Bureau stated yesterday regarding the initial implementation of factory inspections, which are being conducted first in the Hunan District of Shanghai, "The Factory Law is a type of national law, and it has long been implemented in various European and American countries. The first country to implement the Factory Law was the United Kingdom, which was the first country to develop industry. The significance of the Factory Law lies in eliminating the disadvantages that workers experience due to factory life. Therefore, the age of workers, working hours, wage payments, restrictions on child labor and female labor, and factory safety and sanitation equipment are all matters stipulated within the scope of the Factory Law and should be implemented gradually. The significance of the Factory Law is naturally to eliminate the disadvantages that workers experience due to factory life, but factories must not misunderstand that this law is an enemy of factories, or that it is designed to protect workers and increase their bargaining power. Because the original purpose of the Factory Law is to maintain peace between labor and management, eliminate class struggle, and enable capital to develop rationally. Therefore, the purpose of the Factory Law is not so much to protect the interests of workers, but rather to protect the interests of all people in society. If the Factory Law is intended to protect the interests of all people in society, then this law must be fully implemented before it can achieve the practical effect of protection. Otherwise, it will only be equivalent to a kind of decoration. However, when it comes to the implementation of such laws and regulations, it is not enough to simply promulgate the laws and regulations. There must be specially designated personnel who are responsible for supervision in order to seek the realization of the laws and regulations. Therefore, various countries have a factory supervision system, and China also has the establishment of factory inspectors. The establishment of factory inspectors in China is based on the Factory Inspection Law.

Correspondence Between Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Accountants Thoroughly Investigates the Progress of the Inferior Rice Case 147

After receiving a letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce denouncing rice merchants Shu Zhanyuan and Tongxingtai for selling large quantities of inferior rice, it immediately organized a special investigation committee and entrusted accountants Pan Lun and Xu Yongzuo to represent the chamber, along with representatives from the Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes, and Bean Rice Industries Guild and the Rice Industry Guild, to begin investigating the accounts of various rice shops and stores opened by Shu Zhanyuan and Tongxingtai Rice Store to determine whether they had sold inferior rice. It is reported that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to accountants Pan and Xu yesterday, urging them to expedite the investigation. The two accountants also replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, reporting on the progress of the investigation. The drafts of the two letters are disclosed below so that those who are concerned about this matter may know the latest developments.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Letter to Accountants Pan and Xu: Gentlemen, Regarding the case of Shu Zhanyuan and Tongxingtai's private sale of Japanese rice, the matters to be investigated have been entrusted to your accounting firm, together with representatives from the Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes, and Bean Rice Industries Guild and the Rice Industry Guild. The Special Investigation Committee convened its second meeting on the 9th of this month to discuss Tongxingtai's letter requesting exemption from auditing their accounts and requesting approval to ship the rice stored in Yukang. It was decided that a letter should be sent to Tongxingtai instructing them to comply with the notification in this letter and submit all accounts for review before further action is taken. Another letter should be sent to accountants Pan and Xu urging them to complete the investigation of the matters to be investigated in this case as soon as possible. A letter is sent accordingly. Please investigate and expedite the process.

Accountants Pan and Xu's Reply to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: Gentlemen, We have received your letter No. 786 of the General Affairs Department of the 10th of this month, and we have taken note of its contents. Since we received your commission on August 22nd of this year to audit the accounts of the rice firms and Tongtai managed by Shu Zhanyuan, together with representatives from the Bean Rice Industry and the Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Industry Guilds, we immediately dispatched accountants and clerks to work all day. Except for a week-long suspension of work while waiting for your chamber to forward the accounts, we have not interrupted our work to this day. A brief report on the progress of the audit is given below. On August 22nd, after gathering with the representatives from the Bean Rice Industry and the Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Industry Guilds at your chamber, we went to Rentai Three Rice Store, managed by Shu Zhanyuan, and took all the accounts to the Northern City Rice Industry Guild to begin auditing. The work continued until August 28th before it was completed. It was deemed necessary to audit the accounts of Kaitai, Santai, Rentai Company, Jitai Mountain, and Four Rice Shops, which are affiliated to Rentai Three Rice Shop, in detail. Therefore, on August 29th, we sent a letter to your chamber, asking you to inform the four shops and Tongxingtai to send all accounts and documents to your chamber immediately so that we could send staff to audit them. We subsequently received your reply No. 711 of the General Affairs Department and attached 23 books of Jitai, and 5 meetings of Santai accounts. On the 6th of this month, we received your reply No. 721 of the General Affairs Department and attached 6 books of Rentai Company accounts on file. However, Kaitai's accounts have not yet been sent by your chamber, and we do not know why. Upon further investigation, we found that the accounts of the Jitai Mountain, Santai, and Rentai Company rice shops sent by your chamber were incomplete, and no documents were sent. A portion of the accounts of the Jitai Mountain and Rentai Company rice shops has been directly requested from the two rice shops, but the accounts of Santai before March of this year are missing. According to the person in charge of the rice shop, they were lost due to the Shanghai War. Due to the above circumstances, the audit cannot be completed for the time being. We hope that your chamber will immediately inform Kaitai Rice Shop to send all the accounts so that we can complete the report as soon as possible.

The Labor Strike at Qiuxin Factory - Yesterday's News 154

Party and Government Agencies Negotiate a Solution

Workers Held a Membership Meeting Yesterday

According to the Dagong News Agency, work at all departments of the Qiuxin Factory in Nanshi remained suspended yesterday. Party and government agencies believe that the extreme positions taken by both labor and management are inappropriate and, at the request of the Bureau of Public Works, intervened in mediation again.

Party and Government Consultation: At 10:00 AM yesterday, Xue Cixin, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Bureau of Public Works, went to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs to request that they join in mediation. Dai Yongchan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhu Jintao of the Bureau of Social Affairs, and Section Chief Xue met with Wang Chengzong, a member of the Standing Committee of the union, and decided to demand a minimum of two principles: 1. Wages should be paid as usual during the strike period. 2. The dismissed workers should be reinstated without exception. Other conditions should be mediated by party and government agencies after work resumes.

Representative Negotiations: Subsequently, Xue Cixin, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Bureau of Public Works, together with representatives from the party and government, negotiated with the management. The factory's foreman, McTylor, received them. As a result, he agreed to reinstate the dismissed workers, but they would have to be transferred to other departments. As for the wages during the strike period, at most a portion would be paid first. The workers believed that this was a major matter and would have to be approved by all the workers before a decision could be made.

Membership Meeting: The Shipbuilding Industry Union of the First District held a membership meeting at Xinming Lane yesterday at 2:00 PM. Chairman Wang Chengzong reported on: 1. The Bureau of Public Works' floating dock project and the situation of the bureau's section chief coming to discuss the matter. 2. The progress of the strike. The following were discussed: 1. The Bureau of Public Works' floating dock has been affected by the strike. A resolution was passed: A. Appoint Wang Chengzong and Ling Zhangcai to reply to the bureau. B. The contract work for the floating dock will not be delayed for the time being and must be completed before the 16th. 2. Conditions precedent for resuming work: A. All dismissed workers must be reinstated. B. Wages must be paid as usual during the strike period. C. A contract must be revised immediately after work resumes. Workers should not be dismissed during the contract revision period, and union representatives should be rejected. 3. Pass the full text of the revised labor-management contract. 4. If the factory does not recognize the conditions precedent, work will never resume. Meeting adjourned.

Anti-Drug Association Seeking Anti-Drug Songs 157

Selected Entries Will Receive a Large Bonus

The Education Section of the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, in order to promote anti-drug knowledge and expand anti-drug publicity, intends to solicit songs about family anti-drug use to be made into gramophone records for publicity purposes. For example, describe the tragic situation of family opium destruction, the tragedy of young people becoming addicted and falling, and the situation of women sinking into the life of opium addiction. Compose songs that are divided into two paragraphs, each paragraph about three and a half minutes, two paragraphs about seven minutes, enough for one gramophone record. Applicants should first register with the association and submit the composed script for review, and then sing at a scheduled audition. If they are qualified, they will be included in the gramophone record. Each selected song will be awarded a bonus of 200 to 300 yuan. The first solicitation is for six songs. The award is donated by Xu Gong, a member of the executive committee of the association, to show his intention to promote anti-drug publicity.

Disputes Over the Dou and Mi Industry During the Measuring and Grading 158

One Side Keeps Them, One Side Takes Them Away

Rice Merchants Unhappy, Yan and Zhu Resign

The Shanghai Dou and Mi Industry Association held its autumn measuring and grading meeting in the main hall of the Cuixiu Hall of the Yimiao Temple the day before yesterday. It was said that there had been complaints from the industry during the last measuring and grading, so this measuring and grading was extra cautious, and rice merchants from the north and south were invited to the scene to supervise the grading. Before the measuring and grading, a meeting was held to discuss all the methods of measuring and grading, such as punishing any household that violated the rules and regulations, no matter what family. Yan Xiaoquan and Zhu Zixiang, the two executive committee members, were in charge of the measuring and grading. The day before yesterday, on the first day, the measures of each bank were measured and graded. Yan and Zhu found that a certain grain and two rice stores with the most prestige in Nanshi took the lead in violating the rules. At that time, the measurement and grading officer was ordered to temporarily keep the measures of the three stores, and wait for the completion of the measurement and grading before asking the public to review and decide. Then, the buddy of a certain grain store ran to tell the shopkeeper, who sent many shop buddies to rush to the scene, arguing strongly with Yan and Zhu, with a very fierce momentum, and took away the measures. Yan and Zhu tried to stop them because of their responsibility for supervising the measuring and grading, but they were surrounded and were about to use force. The rice merchants from the north and south were very unhappy because such barbarism could not be dealt with, and the executive committee members could not perform their duties in the future, and the rice merchants would also be harmed. They have asked the public association to punish the grain store severely, in order to warn other families to follow suit, and Yan and Zhu resigned from the position of executive committee member to the public association yesterday after being humiliated because they were unable to exercise their duties. It is said that the public association will hold a meeting of the north and south industries to discuss and decide on the handling methods.

At 6 PM yesterday, the Shanghai North Shanghai Business Federation initiated a joint meeting of the Shanghai Road Business Federation (Special Zone 1), the French Concession Business Federation (Special Zone 2), and the Nanshi Business Federation at the Sichuan Road YMCA. Over Two Hundred Stallholders in Zhabei Oppose the Contracted Stall Fee System 163

Petition the Municipal Government to Order Its Immediate Cancellation

According to the Ri Ri News Agency, over two hundred stallholders, including Zhou Changmao in Zhabei, submitted a petition to the Municipal Finance Bureau yesterday, stating: "Presenting a case where local tyrants contract stall fees, forcing stallholders to pay. We respectfully request your review and, on the one hand, send personnel to investigate monopolizing local tyrants, and on the other hand, order the Finance Bureau to cancel the contracted system to relieve the suffering and maintain livelihoods. Since the Shanghai Incident, stallholders have been displaced and their livelihoods have been extremely difficult. Recently, the situation has been relatively peaceful, and the city has gradually recovered, hoping for a way to make a living. Who knew that the local tyrant Yang Dexing would take this opportunity to collude with gentry and officials to contract the stall fees from the Finance Bureau. The contracted monthly fee per stall is only 2 jiao and 7 fen. All the vegetable stalls east of Dayang Bridge, west of Yuyingtang Road, south of Tanjia Bridge, and north of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, a radius of over ten li, must be set up at the Daxing Vegetable Market, and the local tyrant monopolizes it, forcing the monthly fee for vegetarian stalls upstairs to be 2 yuan and 8 jiao, the monthly fee for meat stalls downstairs to be 3 yuan and 5 jiao, and a stall base fee of 5 yuan must be paid. Then, stallholders rely on small capital to make a living, how much can they earn? How can they bear this harsh exploitation? Therefore, all the stallholders have repeatedly petitioned the Fourth District of the Public Security Bureau and Yang Dexing, requesting that in the early days of the city's recovery, small alleys and branch roads where stalls have been set up in the past should still be temporarily set up where they do not hinder traffic, so as to avoid harsh penalties and reduce monthly fees to ease the burden and facilitate business. But in the end, it was ineffective. This kind of exorbitant tax is actually more severe than floods and beasts. How can the common people bear it? If we do not request a strict investigation and cancellation of the contracted system, it will inevitably lead the hawkers to the end, and even prolong the evil power of the local tyrants. Therefore, we are forced to exhaust the situation and humbly request your review and approval for implementation. We are grateful."

Yu A'gen Promoted to Chief Detective of the Chinese Division P] 166

Yu A'gen, the Chinese Chief Detective of the Old Zhabei Police Station, has served in the Public Concession Police Department for over twenty years. Due to his diligence in handling affairs and his repeated success in solving major cases, he has been highly praised by his superiors. Recently, he has solved several major cases in succession, such as the assassination of female fortune teller Wang Wenying, the Xiaoshan kidnapping case, and the flower show case. He has also supervised his subordinates in their efforts to maintain local security. Chief Inspector Qiu Lai has a plan to encourage working personnel and has specially promoted Mr. Yu to Chief Detective of the Chinese Division, who will continue to work at the Old Zhabei Police Station. After receiving the appointment, Mr. Yu is scheduled to take office on the 15th of this month.

Central Bank Inspection Report

No. 136

The 136th inspection report of the Central Bank's issuance reserve states that, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible banknotes of the bank. On September 10, 1932, Wang Yihou, supervisor, conducted the 136th inspection at the bank's Issuing Bureau, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows:

(A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 30,020,422 silver dollars, including 27,082,109 yuan in banknotes and 3,121,913 yuan in subsidiary coins. Total amount of convertible banknote reserves: 30,020,422 silver dollars, including 24,770,022 silver dollars in cash reserves. The cash reserve includes 22,130,354.70 yuan stored in the bank's issuing vault, 1,467,596 yuan stored in branches in various ports, 1,172,071.26 yuan deposited with fellow banks, and 5,434,000 silver dollars converted from guarantee reserves.

(B) Total amount of customs gold convertible banknotes issued: 425,000 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold convertible banknote reserves: 425,000 customs gold units. The reserve includes 170,000 US dollars deposited with fellow banks in the local port, which is equivalent to 425,000 customs gold units at a fixed price of 0.40. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's Exchange Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations.

This report is hereby submitted.

September 10, 1932, Supervisory Board of the Central Bank.

China Industrial Bank Issuance Reserve Report

No. 13

The China Industrial Bank's Issuing Department's reserve has always been completely separated from the business department's funds, and the reserve is fully available. The issuance reserve figures for September 10, 1932, are announced as follows:

Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 21,160,851 yuan, including 13,715,851 yuan issued by the bank, 3,653,000 yuan issued by affiliated banks, and 4,240,000 yuan used by various firms.

Except for the portion used by various firms, which is inspected according to the original method, this inspection covers the issuance amount of convertible banknotes by the bank and affiliated banks, totaling 17,368,851 yuan. The reserve amount for convertible banknotes by the bank and affiliated banks is 17,368,851 yuan, including 10,561,651 yuan in cash reserve and 6,807,200 yuan in guarantee reserve. The cash reserve accounts for over 60% and the guarantee reserve accounts for less than 40%, all of which have been inspected and found to be accurate.

The inspector is Xie Lin, CPA of Zhengze Accounting Firm.

Rope Manufacturing Trade Association

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the 26th meeting of the Executive Committee was held. Chairman Fei Rusheng presided over the meeting and performed the usual formalities.

1. The chairman reported that the Samsung Printing Bureau had leased a portion of the association's office as an office space with a monthly rent of 10 yuan, which had been leased on August 6. A motion was made for ratification, and it was resolved to ratify it.

2. The chairman reported that, according to the report from member Xie Ji Rope Factory, 20 rope machines were sold last month on the 27th. A request was made to reduce the factory's monthly donation by 4 yuan starting from September and to send someone to investigate. A motion was made for a resolution, and it was resolved to send committee member Zhang Jinshan to investigate and reply to the reduction.

3. The chairman proposed that the Da Zhonghua Rope Factory sold 509 catties of rope to Kang Yuan Canning Factory at a reduced price. It was resolved at the 24th Executive Committee meeting to impose a penalty in accordance with the regulations. Later, the Kang Yuan Factory sent a letter stating that the Da Zhonghua Rope Factory did not sell at a low price, and the Hua Tong Rope Factory reported to the association that it was a misunderstanding. A motion was made to decide whether to cancel the case, and it was resolved to have the documentation department send a letter to the Kang Yuan Factory for a reply.

4. The chairman reported that the association's business rules have now been drafted and should be revised. A motion was made for a resolution, and it was resolved to slightly revise the original draft, mimeograph it, and distribute it to the executive committee members for consideration, and then make a decision at the 27th Executive Committee meeting.

5. A motion was made on how to handle the matter, and it was resolved to have the documentation department send a stern letter of reminder.

6. Committee member Zhang Jinshan proposed that the Hua Da Rope Factory sold 143 catties of rope to Long Xingchang Wool Store at a reduced price, violating the association's regulations. Zheng Zhengqiu and Hu Die to Perform Tomorrow

Zheng Zhengqiu, a veteran of the new drama scene, has been focusing on directing work since entering the film industry and has not performed on stage for a long time. At the request of the local people, he and Hu Die performed a temporarily composed satirical play, "Candidate Wife," which was highly praised. National Goods Factory Association Solicits Samples and Trademarks

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association sent a letter to various factories yesterday requesting them to send their trademarks and samples to the association for forwarding to Guangdong. The letter reads: "Dear Sirs, Recently, Ma Huayi, representative of the Guangdong People's National Salvation Association, came to Shanghai to investigate the seizure of goods from the Jiuji Cane Factory. Because the goods from various Shanghai factories are sold to Guangdong Province and are sometimes mistakenly seized, the association sent personnel to accompany Representative Ma to visit various factories in person to avoid misunderstandings. However, due to time constraints, they were unable to visit all the factories, which is regrettable. Now, Zhang Zilian, standing committee member of the association, is scheduled to go to Guangdong on official business on the 19th of this month. We received a telegram from Representative Ma requesting Zhang to bring all the samples and trademarks of national goods manufacturers to Guangdong for review to avoid future seizures. We are concerned about the promotion of national goods and hereby inform your factory that if you have goods sold in Guangzhou, please list the trademarks and outer carton markings separately and send them along with samples and address information to the association before the 17th of this month so that Zhang can bring them with him to avoid future seizures. This matter is of great importance to the interests of all factories. Please do not neglect it."

Letter

Dear Editor, I have just read a news item in the "Local News" column of your newspaper dated September 12th, regarding a fraud case involving impersonating an inspector. The article stated that Lei Wenkui claimed in the Fourth Criminal Court of the Special District Court that he had obtained a position as an inspector at the Fisheries Administration Bureau, and Dong Bin also claimed to be an inspector on a boat of the Fisheries Administration Bureau. This is shocking. After investigation, there is no position of "inspector" under the jurisdiction of this bureau, nor has Lei Wenkui or Dong Bin been appointed as inspectors. The two criminals dared to borrow the name to carry out their fraudulent tricks, which is extremely illegal. In addition to sending a letter to the Special District Court requesting that they be severely punished in accordance with the law to deter others, we hereby request that you investigate and make a correction to uphold public justice. Sincerely, Jiangzhe District Marine Fisheries Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, September 16th.

Dear Editor, I have just read a news item on the fourth page of your newspaper dated September 12th, 1932, regarding the Women's Relief Association reorganizing its affairs. My name is listed in the article. I formally resigned from the Municipal Party Department and the Women's Relief Association in November 1932, and my resignation was approved at that time, and I was relieved of my concurrent duties. Since Xiaoying has resigned, she has no right to interfere. Your newspaper's publication of my name is inconsistent with the facts. Please make a correction. Wang Xiaoying respectfully submits, September 12th.

Editor, In the news column of your newspaper dated the 12th of this month, there was a report about two nephews accusing their uncle of embezzling property, namely Wenrong et al. suing their uncle Yuchen for embezzling public property. The facts described in the report needlessly involve family matters and are quite painful. There is an unavoidable bitter reason for the lawsuit that has now occurred, but this is a minor matter of property infringement between individuals and is not important news. We hope that you will publish this in the "Letters to the Editor" column. Xu Wenrong and Xu Wenxin respectfully submit.

Supplement to Local News of Shen Bao

Empty Words and Shadows by Yan Xuying

Buddha

Tea houses are called "Little Dharma Halls" because tea drinkers never get involved in anything, so their criticisms are relatively fair. However, the situation in Shanghai's tea houses is different. Suppose two parties want to go to a tea house to "drink tea and talk," they must first invite several tycoons and a few thugs. If you get a tycoon to help, you can save face even if your reasons are insufficient. Otherwise, even if your reasons are perfectly valid, you will be defeated. It is a dream to expect the gentlemen invited to drink tea to come out and say a few fair words.

The League of Nations is like a tea house, and China and Japan are like friends of parties A and B drinking tea and talking. Now, party A is unable to resist on its own and cannot get a tycoon to help. It is futile to rely on a few tea-drinking gentlemen to come out and "right the wrongs" and say a few fair words. Even if there are a few who come out to uphold justice, but party B's attitude is tough and unwilling to listen, it is just empty talk and will never be effective.

According to a London dispatch yesterday, the Observer's commentary stated that in recent days, there has been much speculation about the Lytton Report. "A clever diplomat will surely intend to give Japan substance and China shadows." Originally, in any matter, if you are unwilling to shed some sweat and blood and unwilling to sacrifice yourself, but only hope that others will sacrifice and only hope that others will uphold justice, there is no such principle in the world.

What is a shadow? A shadow is something that is intangible and cannot be grasped. Tell me, what is the use of emptiness without a real impression when the reality is gone? A child is beaten and cries. An adult comes out from the side and says, "Don't cry, go back home. I'll get revenge for you. I'll beat him up." The child cries and goes home. The impression in his mind is still that an adult will help him.

The west wind brings sorrow to Jiangnan, turning back to a world unbearable,

The officials of Taiwan Province have a corpse-like air, singing and dancing in peace are drunken dreams,

The willow camp is filled with charming butterflies at night, military reports from the border enter the wild silkworms,

The banana trees in the old courtyard are as green as before, the broken doors lock in the cold ashes day after day.

Scientific Charcoal Manufacturing Method by Tian Lan

In the electric current, charcoal is most needed. Our country buys it from foreign countries every year, and a considerable amount of money flows out. Moreover, most of the charcoal sold on the market is foreign goods. If we do not engage in manufacturing, how can we stop this leakage?

The ordinary charcoal manufacturing method is extremely simple. As long as you have a little knowledge, you can manufacture it according to the law, and the capital is small and the profit is large. With a small capital of one or two thousand gold, you can start a small charcoal factory.

The main raw materials of charcoal are coke dust, coke, flour, sugar water, and clean water. These four things are not expensive, so making charcoal is sure to make money.

When making it, choose pure coke dust, pound it into an extremely fine powder with a pestle, sieve it with a fine sieve, add one-eighth or one-sixth of dry flour, mix it evenly, and adjust it with suitable light sugar water. Seal it for two or three hours to prevent moisture from escaping. After the charcoal powder is thoroughly moistened, use a mold to make charcoal sheets and charcoal strips.

Then move these charcoal sheets and charcoal strips to the stove and bake them with a low fire to gradually dry them. Gradually increase the heat from time to time. Once they are completely dry, put them in an iron box, cover them with a layer of coke dust to prevent exposure to the air, and let them burn naturally.

Then move them to a cool place, wait for them to cool thoroughly, take them out, add sugar juice, and boil them in water for 30 minutes. Then dry them in the same way as before. After burning and refining two or three times, the sheets and strips are firm and become usable charcoal. However, it is slightly inferior to machine-made charcoal.

Social Improvement Discussion Group: My Observation of Early Marriage by A Yan

Is early marriage harmful?

Zeng Kan has published articles on early marriage by Huanhua and Wenbing successively. Huanhua focuses on explaining the evils of early marriage; Wenbing focuses on analyzing the causes of early marriage and its remedial measures. My personal opinion is not entirely the same as theirs. I believe that there is indeed a phenomenon of early marriage in China today, but the so-called early marriage is no longer a problem. Early marriage may cause some evils in certain respects, but it is relative rather than absolute.

Wenbing's observation of the causes of early marriage is very clear, and my meaning is roughly the same as his. The occurrence of the phenomenon of early marriage in China is primarily based on the family system left over from feudal society. Second, the widespread phenomenon of early marriage mostly occurs in self-sufficient agricultural societies and in times when it is relatively easy to make a living.

However, due to the shift in trends, these explanations can no longer be applied to recent times. Although family organizations are still struggling, these organizations will be washed away by the new torrent. In the vast rural society, except for a very small number of landlords and rich peasants, most are living in bankruptcy and displacement, and they have no time to take care of themselves, let alone talk about early marriage. Similarly, in cities, the middle and upper classes have the ability to marry early, but because their sons have received modern education, they are obsessed with so-called free love. Parents have long lost their control over marriage. The urban proletariat lives in instability and has no possibility of early marriage. In this way, even if there are still some exceptional cases of early marriage at present, the phenomenon of early marriage is gradually declining, and the so-called early marriage is no longer a problem.

The objective environment has reduced the phenomenon of early marriage among the Chinese people. But we cannot deny that there is still a phenomenon of early marriage in poor and remote cities and towns, especially in the social strata of farmers and small farmers and above. Here we might as well discuss whether early marriage itself has any evils, and what is the degree of evils?

Most people think that early marriage is the biggest loss in terms of physical fitness, but that is not entirely true. The main thing is to see how well the person concerned has developed. Some people think that early marriage can remedy the problem of youth masturbation. Most young men and women over the age of fifteen have committed this illegal problem. (The results of the examination of the dormitories in Jiangsu Zhenzhong show that more than 70% of the quilts have traces of sperm.) Rather than illegal ejaculation, if the environment permits, it is better to marry early.

Secondly, some people worry about the economic problems after early marriage. In my opinion, this is not a problem, because fundamentally, the occurrence of early marriage depends on his own economic environment. If the economic environment permits, nothing will be a problem. People who have concerns about economic childbirth have no possibility of early marriage. In small and medium-sized farmer families, they believe that getting their children married early not only does not have economic concerns, but can also get workers who do not need wages, and marrying a daughter-in-law will increase their production.

So my conclusion is:

The phenomenon of early marriage rises and falls with social changes. Early marriage is gradually decreasing at present, and the so-called early marriage will no longer be a problem in the future. We don't have to say for sure that early marriage is not good, but we don't have to advocate early marriage. In the future, the union of the sexes can be left to nature.

Why the Slave of Love by Wu

My wife is the same every day. After lunch, she goes to the hospital to visit her close friend Suxin, and Suxin also waits eagerly for my wife's arrival after lunch every day. Obviously, they have been firmly connected by a solemn friendship and have deepened the interest in life.

But today my wife came back with a heavy sorrow, which surprised me very much, so I asked her in a low voice, and she said:

"Alas! I think it's really boring to be a woman. What's the meaning of someone like Suxin?

When I approached her bed today, she was talking with her fourteen-year-old younger sister with tears in their eyes. Of course, I suddenly felt that there must be a major misfortune between them, but I had to sit down silently, in order to find a way to comfort her with a quiet attitude. Sure enough, when her sister left, she held my hands tightly, and tears fell one after another.

"Do you know, there is really no one in the world more miserable than me." She cried and said: "Just now my younger sister told me that my husband actually stayed in my house for two nights with a woman I didn't know, and also gave her a cheongsam I had just made not long ago."

At this time, her throat seemed to be blocked by a stone, and she couldn't say anything more. So I quickly comforted her and said:

"Suxin! Don't worry, for your lovely children, for your postpartum body, be more optimistic. At the same time, this may be a temporary mistake of your husband's, and he will definitely change in the future."

After that, she continued sobbing and said:

"No, you have overestimated him too much, he will definitely not regret it. You know him completely. You know that I have been married to him for four years, and for three years he has not taken care of the family affairs at all, even though he is always idle at home. Of course, for the sake of life, I have to continue to be my elementary school teacher, maintain myself, maintain the family, and also support him in smoking and playing cards. Of course, I don't hope to ask my husband for gratitude for this, but I never thought that when I was in confinement, he would have the heart to make friends with other women and have carnal relations. This is an extremely fierce blow to me."

"But," I said, "you should think like this: We can give him a chance, because some men sometimes do things they don't want to do. If you can move him with such pure love, even if he has an iron heart, he will one day be grateful to you."

After that, she said again:

"He doesn't want to do anything, he's just too lazy, if I don't work he will starve to death. Of course, I absolutely don't want to depend on my husband for life, as long as I have a glimmer of hope. However, the little money I earn with hard work, if he can use it very sparingly, it doesn't matter, but every day he either plays at the Great World or brings many people to my house to play cards, so when I come back from teaching, I still have to cook for them, which is extremely tiring. At the same time, he still has a wife before, and now they still come and go often, calling her 'Eighth Sister' in a disgusting way. Do you think it's so meaningless for me to suffer like this!"

Then I asked:

"Why did he want to marry you when he already had a wife?"

"They're divorced."

"Then why do they still come and go so affectionately?"

"Only God knows."

We talked for a long time, and I really felt bad for her. At the same time, she told me that she had resigned from the original elementary school because of giving birth to a child, and now she is going to work as a proofreader at XX News through a friend's introduction, even before she is a month postpartum. I think this is so unsuitable for a postpartum body, but what can I do? Therefore, a woman like her is really a slave to her husband!"

My wife was still sighing endlessly after she finished speaking, and I was also silent.

Xiaoshan Kidnappers Arrested in Shanghai 167

Rescued Hostage Cao A'yu

All Kidnappers to be Transferred

Unexpectedly, the plan was discovered by Detective Yu A'gen of the Zhabei Police Station, who then led Detectives Liu Junqing, Wang Yingjie, Chen Yonggui, and Bao Detective Chen Xikang to arrest the three kidnappers Wang, Li, and Zhu at No. 5 Rongqing Lane, Robison Road. Accomplices Chen Miaoqian, Gao Cailang, Shen Baohe, Yang Bingwen, and others were also arrested, and the hostage Cao A'yu was rescued. Wang Zhou, who was watching the hostage, was also brought back to the police station and sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide held a continued hearing. The police station's lawyer, Ru BaoYi, stated that although the location of the arrest was in Shanghai, the crime scene was inland. Now, the Zhejiang Provincial Security Department has sent personnel to the case for investigative convenience and requested a transfer, which the police station does not oppose. Subsequently, Deputy Officer Shi of the Security Department submitted an official document requesting the transfer of the eight suspects, including Wang Ziqing. Judge Feng reviewed the report and ordered that the eight suspects, including Wang Ziqing, along with the hostage Cao A'yu, be handed over to the representatives of the Zhejiang Security Department to be taken back for trial.

Ye-Xu Lawsuit Temporarily Suspended 168

Pending Civil Court Decision Before Resuming Trial

The case of Ye Lishao suing Xu JiPing for bigamy and fraud was scheduled for a continued hearing yesterday. Around 2 p.m., men and women flocked to the court to listen. After the judge took the bench and finished hearing other cases, this case was then examined. However, although the presiding judge had previously decided in court that the lawsuit between Xu JiPing and Hu Bingheng in the civil court must be resolved before investigating Ye's accusations against Xu, the civil court dispute has not yet resumed. This case is still difficult to proceed. The presiding judge then informed both parties that the civil case was scheduled to resume on September 28th, and this case should still follow the previous decision and be heard again after the civil court's ruling. However, the lawyer for the plaintiff, Ye Lishao, requested that the facts be reviewed as the witnesses were all present. The presiding judge then informed the lawyer that, regarding the charge of bigamy, it must be proven that the defendant's other marriage was a formal union before the charge of bigamy could be established. Which union, Xu with Ye or Hu, came first, and which was the official marriage, all should be based on the civil court's decision. Therefore, this case cannot be opened for trial now. After the judge finished speaking, a written order was issued to suspend the trial proceedings. The plaintiff, the defendant, and their lawyers then left in succession, and the onlookers dispersed.

Baoshan Long-Distance Bus Increases Service 170

Increased from Seven to Eleven Trips

Each trip connects with trains and ferries

The Baoshan City-Songjiang-Liuhang long-distance bus service operated by the Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company, originally scheduled to run seven times a day, was put into operation the day before yesterday. It is now learned that the company has been ordered by the municipal government to increase the number of daily trips by four, for a total of eleven. Baoshan to Wusong: first trip at 7:30 a.m., 9:00 a.m., 10:22 a.m., 11:00 a.m., 12:25 p.m., 1:05 p.m., 2:12 p.m., 3:00 p.m., 3:55 p.m., 5:00 p.m., 5:40 p.m. Wusong to Baoshan: first trip at 8:40 a.m., 9:20 a.m., 10:42 a.m., 11:20 a.m., 12:47 p.m., 1:23 p.m., 2:32 p.m., 3:20 p.m., 4:17 p.m., 5:20 p.m., 6:02 p.m. Yangxing to Wusong: first trip at 7:30 a.m., 9:00 a.m., 10:22 a.m., 11:00 a.m., 12:25 p.m., 1:05 p.m., 2:12 p.m., 3:00 p.m., 3:55 p.m., 5:00 p.m., 5:40 p.m. Wusong to Yangxing: first trip at 8:40 a.m., 9:20 a.m., 10:42 a.m., 11:20 a.m., 12:47 p.m., 1:23 p.m., 2:32 p.m., 3:20 p.m., 4:17 p.m., 5:20 p.m., 6:02 p.m. Yangxing to Liuhang: first trip at 9:00 a.m., 11:00 a.m., 1:05 p.m., 2:50 p.m., 4:35 p.m. Liuhang to Yangxing: first trip at 9:45 a.m., 11:45 a.m., 1:50 p.m., 3:40 p.m., 5:25 p.m. The first, third, fifth, seventh, ninth, and eleventh trips, except for Yangxing to Liuhang and Liuhang to Yangxing, all connect with train schedules, and the bus waits at the train station. The second, fourth, sixth, eighth, and tenth trips all connect with the municipal government's ferry schedules, and the bus waits at the ferry terminal. If the train or ferry is delayed, the bus departure time will be slightly delayed, but not exceeding ten minutes. Those traveling from Baoshan to Yangxing or from Yangxing to Baoshan must get off at the Sanguantang Station and transfer. It is also heard that the company will expand greatly in the future. In addition to the current routes from Shanghai to Taicang, Liuhang Town, Jiading, and Baoshan, it will expand its routes to Taicang City and then to Changshu. It has already applied to the Provincial Government Construction Department for approval and is in the planning process, with a budget of 1.2 million yuan.
